[<p class="c-meta__more">\n</p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">It\u2019s been 25 years since <a data-tag="r-kelly" href="https://variety.com/t/r-kelly/" id="auto-tag_r-kelly">R. Kelly</a> first had to answer for sexual abuse allegations. Two and a half decades of new reports, new witnesses, new testimonies, new windows into an age-old story of powerful men seizing the chance to play God while trampling countless women \u2014 girls \u2014 into the dirt. And yet, as a devastating new docuseries lays out in damning detail, Kelly has nonetheless found a way to evade the charges and any real consequences almost every time.</span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">In six hour-long chapters, Lifetime\u2019s \u201c<a data-tag="surviving-r-kelly" href="https://variety.com/t/surviving-r-kelly/" id="auto-tag_surviving-r-kelly">Surviving R. Kelly</a>\u201d is perhaps the most comprehensive dive into the terrible, tangled history of allegations against the singer yet. The first two episodes dig into his childhood, in which he both was recognized as a musical prodigy and sexually abused himself and his unstoppable rise to stardom, and his relationship to Aaliyah, whom he met when she was just 12 years old. The third and fourth episodes detail the circumstances of the so-called \u201cpee tape,\u201d which allegedly showed Kelly having sex with and urinating on a 14 year-old girl, and the subsequent child pornography case that ended in a surprise acquittal. The final two episodes highlight the reports from the last several years that Kelly has isolated and groomed women and girls into a sex cult for his own pleasure. </span></p>, <p> <div class="admz" id="adm-inline-article-ad-1">\n<div class="adma google-publisher" data-device="Desktop" data-width="300">\n<div class="pmc-adm-goog-pub-div ad-text">\n<div class="ad-rotatable adw-300 adh-250" id="gpt-variety-article-mid-article-uid0"></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<section class="c-related c-related--review">\n<h3 class="c-heading c-heading--related">More Reviews</h3>\n<article class="c-card c-card--focus-featured" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">\n<figure class="c-card__image" itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" style="background-image:url('https://pmcvariety.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/the-vanishing-keepers.jpg?w=700&amp;h=393&amp;crop=1');">\n<a class="" href="https://variety.com/2019/film/reviews/the-vanishing-review-1203097498/">\n<img alt="'The Vanishing' Review" itemprop="contentUrl" src="https://pmcvariety.files.wordpress.com/2019/01/the-vanishing-keepers.jpg?w=700&amp;h=393&amp;crop=1"/>\n</a>\n</figure>\n<header class="c-card__header">\n<h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="headline">\n<a href="https://variety.com/2019/film/reviews/the-vanishing-review-1203097498/">Film Review: 'The Vanishing'</a>\n</h3>\n</header>\n</article>\n</section>\n</p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">All of these incidents have been exhaustively reported and dissected in public. Women have come forward with eyewitness accounts of gaslighting, intimidation, molestation, violence. There\u2019s so much smoke surrounding Kelly at this point that he might as well be walking around fully engulfed in flames. This much, even to Kelly\u2019s most stubborn defenders, has finally become obvious. And despite some recent explosive reports of Kelly\u2019s allegedly ongoing sexual abuse, \u201cSurviving <a data-tag="r-kelly" href="https://variety.com/2019/tv/news/surviving-r-kelly-will-air-despite-legal-threat-1203098870/" id="related_article_link_r-kelly">R. Kelly</a>\u201d is arguably the most prominent strike against him yet. </span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">But what makes this docuseries so crucial beyond its singularity is its dogged insistence on indicting not just Kelly, but everyone in the music industry and beyond who have allegedly enabled him. As one survivor puts it, \u201cthe reason why he could do it is because he had people helping him\u201d \u2014 and as \u201c<a data-tag="surviving-r-kelly" href="https://variety.com/2018/tv/news/surviving-r-kelly-docu-drea-kelly-lisa-van-allen-brie-miranda-bryant-interview-1203088434/" id="related_article_link_surviving-r-kelly">Surviving R. Kelly</a>\u201d convincingly argues, he still does to this day. It\u2019s a stark, horrifying reminder that merely saying \u201cTime\u2019s Up\u201d for abuse doesn\u2019t mean it is, and that fighting sexual violence means fighting a system explicitly built to minimize it whenever possible.</span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">Aside from some dramatic musical stings and fades to black, the docuseries mostly eschews salacious framing in favor of measured, thorough documentation and extensive interviews with people from every stage of Kelly\u2019s life. We hear from Kelly\u2019s targets, bear witness to their startlingly similar accounts of abuse, watch them blink back tears as they try to make us understand why they\u2019re speaking out. Driving home just how long this pattern has been playing out is the fact that while some of the survivors are young still, others now have daughters older than they were when they first met Kelly.</span></p>, <p> <div class="admz" id="adm-inline-article-ad-2">\n<div class="adma google-publisher" data-device="Desktop" data-width="300">\n<div class="pmc-adm-goog-pub-div ad-text">\n<div class="ad-rotatable adw-300 adh-250" id="gpt-dsk-tab-mid-article2-uid1"></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">We also hear from the survivors\u2019 friends, coaches, teachers, siblings. We hear from their parents, some of whom remain desperate to hear from their daughters for the first time in years. We even hear from Kelly\u2019s own brothers, producers, and employees, watching them grapple in real time with their own culpability in protecting him over the years. </span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">The testimonies are wrenching and furious, brimming over with pain, regret, and determination. And all of them, in one way or another, tell the same story of a brilliant and charismatic man taking every inch of power he got and using it to systematically exploit black women and girls, because he knew he could.</span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">What\u2019s more, \u201cSurviving R. Kelly\u201d also brings in journalists, culture writers, clinical psychologists, sexual violence experts, and even Kelly\u2019s industry peers to help explain how he\u2019s dodged 25 years of steadily piling evidence. Insight on how Kelly balanced two disparate sides of his musical personality \u2014 from the sex-obsessed player who dropped \u201cBump \u2018n Grind\u201d to the wholesome church ready anthem singer of \u201cI Believe I Can Fly\u201d \u2014 makes clear how he and the industry compartmentalized his professional prowess against the constant chaos of his personal life. </span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">Context on how initial reports framed Kelly\u2019s marriage to 15 year-old Aaliyah and alleged \u201csex tape\u201d involving a 14 year-old (translation: tape of a sexual assault) reveals how unprepared, or unwilling, many were to call out abuse when faced with it. Clinical research, explained by experts with clear-cut patience, sheds light on how Kelly continues to attract women and girls into his orbit despite a quarter-century\u2019s worth of meticulously documented horrors. In these ways, the docuseries seems to both anticipate the Kelly camp\u2019s rebuttals and work to preemptively disprove them, shattering pushback with the blunt force of logic.</span></p>, <p><span style="font-weight:400;">\u201cSurviving R. Kelly\u201d isn\u2019t an easy watch; I dreaded pressing play. But once I started, it was impossible to look away \u2014 which is as it should be. It\u2019s been too easy for too many to avert their eyes when the truth was staring back all along.</span></p>, <p> <div class="admz" id="adm-inline-article-ad-x-9">\n<div class="adma google-publisher" data-device="Desktop" data-width="300">\n<div class="pmc-adm-goog-pub-div ad-text">\n<div class="ad-rotatable adw-300 adh-250" id="gpt-variety-article-mid-articleX-uid2"></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</p>, <p><i><span style="font-weight:400;">\u201cSurviving R. Kelly\u201d airs January 2, 3, and 4 on Lifetime at 9 pm EST.</span></i></p>, <p>TV Review: 'Surviving R. Kelly'</p>, <p>When \u201cThe Titan Games\u201d premieres Thursday on NBC, it will mark more than yet another addition to the Dwayne Johnson oeuvre. The athletic competition series \u2014 which features the erstwhile Rock as exec producer and host \u2014 is a central piece of an evolving unscripted strategy at television\u2019s reigning top-rated network. That strategy was front [...]</p>, <p>In today\u2019s TV news roundup, BBC America announced the premiere date for Season 2 of \u201cKilling Eve\u201d and Comedy Central released a new trailer for Season 2 of \u201cCorporate.\u201d DATES More Reviews Film Review: 'The Vanishing' The second season of Marvel\u2019s \u201cThe Punisher\u201d is set to premiere Jan. 18 on Netflix. Kelly,\u201d will air beginning tonight as planned despite a legal threat from the singer, a rep for the network told Variety. \u201cLifetime has always been a brand that champions women\u2019s stories,\u201d the statement reads.\xa0\u201cThe documentary will air as scheduled, starting tonight at 9pm ET/PT.\u201d More Reviews Film Review: [...]</p>, <p>William Arkin has created articles and reports for NBC News and The Los Angeles Times, among other media venues. [<p>In anticipation of the 20th anniversary of the death of John F. Kennedy Jr., ABC tonight will air <em>The Last Days of JFK Jr</em>. \xa0\u2014 a\xa0documentary featuring interviews and previously unseen video about Kennedy and his wife, Carolyn Bessette-Kennedy, <a href="https://people.com/politics/they-would-love-hard-and-they-would-fight-hard-inside-the-passionate-marriage-of-jfk-jr-and-carolyn-bessette-kennedy/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">both of whom died in a plane crash on July 16, 1999</a>.</p>, <p>We talked to executive producer Terri Lichstein about what to expect from the special, and whether the images will make us sad all over again.</p>, <p><strong>ENTERTAINMENT WEEKLY: Was this a difficult project? When did you begin?</strong><br/>\n<strong>TERRI LICHSTEIN:</strong> We actually have been looking at this for a while, over the last year or two, collecting these special interviews. What the documentary really does is take a look at his life. At every stage of his life, there are these voices that pull us into who he was and then eventually what happens to him at the end of his life. I love how in the beginning of his story, we talk to his nanny and the Secret Service man who was around him and into high school. We talk to high school friends, two of his college friends, his past girlfriends. Then there was <a href="https://ew.com/article/2016/07/29/cindy-crawford-jfk-jr-documentary-outtake/">the <em>George</em> period</a>, before we get to the day that he died and the whole flight.\xa0This is a very intimate look at his life. We made a very unique arrangement with a photographer we found. When I first sat down and I talked to the producing team, I looked at the material and was like, \u201cI don\u2019t remember that shot.\u201d We really had an opportunity to spend a lot of time with this material and really incorporate it into this entire story.</p>, <p class="tempo-iframe-embed-container"><iframe aspect_ratio="56.25%" class="tempo-iframe-embed" height="360" scrolling="no" src="https://wpcomwidgets.com?width=640&amp;height=360&amp;frameborder=0&amp;style&amp;class&amp;scrolling=no&amp;webkitallowfullscreen&amp;mozallowfullscreen&amp;allowfullscreen&amp;resize=0&amp;replace_attributes=1&amp;fallback=%3Cp+class%3D%22protected-embed-fallback%22%3EThis+embed+is+invalid%3C%2Fp%3E&amp;_data=PGlmcmFtZSBzcmM9Imh0dHBzOi8vYWJjbmV3cy5nby5jb20vdmlkZW8vZW1iZWQ%2FaWQ9NTk4ODY5OTgiIHdpZHRoPSI2NDAiIGhlaWdodD0iMzYwIiBzY3JvbGxpbmc9Im5vIiBzdHlsZT0iYm9yZGVyOm5vbmU7IiBhbGxvd2Z1bGxzY3JlZW49IiIgZnJhbWVib3JkZXI9IjAiIGNsYXNzPSIiIHJlc2l6ZT0iMCIgcmVwbGFjZV9hdHRyaWJ1dGVzPSIxIj48L2lmcmFtZT4%3D%2C4accc0d38c9dcee52bf0f2529372100f7e27232f&amp;_tag=protected-iframe&amp;_hash=f91db6f2193143f16063b214f32bd898" width="640"></iframe></p>, <p><strong>Was it a mistake for him to fly that night?</strong><br/>\n                  Oh boy, I can\u2019t really be the one to answer that question. I think in the documentary, you get a feeling from two pilots who we interviewed, one of whom decided not to fly on that night and another who did decide to fly that night. They both realized the conditions were really bad. I think in the film, you get the feeling that, boy, wouldn\u2019t it have been great if they had decided to go the next day?</p>, <p><strong>Is this going to make viewers sad?</strong><br/>\n                  There\u2019s a combination of emotions when you watch this film. There\u2019s a sense of fulfillment and happiness and the incredible man that he turned out to be. Also there\u2019s the loss that everybody feels that he never got to fulfill his life. At the end of the film, there is this great quote that he gives us when he\u2019s talking about his father. I love it: \u201cOne of the reasons why he remains a figure that captures our imagination is that his life was uncompleted, and his work was uncompleted. There is that sense of promises that were left by circumstances undone.\u201d Here we have this man telling us about a life cut short, which is his father, and he ended up in exactly the same position.</p>, <p><em>The Last Days of JFK Jr.</em> airs at 9 p.m. ET tonight on ABC.</p>]
[<p class="entry-meta"><time class="entry-time" datetime="2019-01-03T03:56:01+00:00">3rd January 2019</time> by <span class="entry-author"><a class="entry-author-link" href="https://www.monstersandcritics.com/author/anita-smith/" rel="author"><span class="entry-author-name">Anita Smith</span></a></span></p>, <p>Season 2 of the FOX hit <a href="https://www.fox.com/gordon-ramsays-24-hours-to-hell-and-back/">Gordon Ramsay\u2019s 24 Hours to Hell and Back</a> premiered tonight, and his first stop was The Big Easy: <a href="https://www.monstersandcritics.com/smallscreen/the-trolley-stop-cafe-story-behind-popular-new-orleans-restaurant-on-gordon-ramsays-24-hours-to-hell-and-back/">The Trolley Stop Cafe</a> in New Orleans.</p>, <p>We first meet the restaurant owner, <a href="https://www.monstersandcritics.com/tag/ragnar/" title="Ragnar">Ragnar</a>, who bought the restaurant from his grandfather to keep it a family-owned establishment, draining his savings account in the process. According to Darrin, the kitchen manager, Ragnar doesn\u2019t have the experience to run a restaurant (he was previously an energy consultant), and he\u2019s hardly ever there. Ragnar admits to working from home a lot since he feels his job is mostly paperwork.</p>, <p>Darren thinks poorly of Ragnar, and since Ragnar\u2019s never around, he doesn\u2019t seem to notice. But he is aware enough that he knows sales are declining, and something has to give.</p>, <p>\u201cIf I don\u2019t make this restaurant work, I know that the family legacy will end with me.\u201d</p>, <p>Keeping in line with the show format, Gordon\u2019s team comes in to hide cameras around the restaurant. And since Gordon knows businesses tend to be on their best behavior when he\u2019s around, he\u2019s got to go undercover \u2026 as a cop!</p>, <p>Gordon meets up with actual deputies and they all ride over to The Trolley Stop Cafe together. He finds out that deputies eat at a discount at The Trolley Stop, but that\u2019s not enough to motivate law enforcement from going there. Once they sit down the eat, the three order nachos, fried oysters, a seafood omelet, and a pecan waffle.</p>, <p>Gordon notices there\u2019s no manager in sight. More than half an hour later, their food is ready.</p>, <p>Gordon notices the nacho cheese is rancid, possibly spoiled. He spits out his food immediately and pleads with the officers not to eat the food.</p>, <p>\u201cThis is some of the most disgusting food I\u2019ve ever seen,\u201d he pronounced. And he\u2019s seen more than his fair share of disgusting food.</p>, <p>(Viewer discretion advised. Those with weak or sensitive stomachs, don\u2019t even click.)</p>, <p><div class="rll-youtube-player" data-id="qb4D17Ms1p8" data-query="start=2&amp;feature=oembed"></div><noscript><iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/qb4D17Ms1p8?start=2&amp;feature=oembed" width="500"></iframe></noscript></p>, <p>Enough\u2019s enough. The gauntlet napkin has been thrown down and the deputy outfit is off. Gordon emerges from what appears to be a supply closet as himself, in full WTF mode. First things first: Time to announce to the patrons that they are eating utter garbage!</p>, <p>Gordon asks for the restaurant staff to come out and show themselves and notices someone is missing.</p>, <p>\u201cThe owner\u2019s not here? Why?\u201d demands Gordon.</p>, <p>\u201cHe\u2019s a sheltered boy who lives with his parents and manages us through cell phones,\u201d answers Darren.</p>, <p>Gordon tells patrons to stop eating, leave the restaurant (group dine and dash!), and join him in the parking lot for some hard truths. Time to watch the video footage!</p>, <p>Cameras unveil staff snapping at each other, a beyond-disgusting kitchen, open containers, flies on food, and finished food sitting on dirty grills. The staff is horrified and the patrons look nauseous (and rightfully so). \u201cI\u2019ll never come here again,\u201d one woman declares.</p>, <p>Meanwhile,\xa0Ragnar shows up in a cop car, for some reason, and Gordon lays into him. Gordon finds out that Ragnar is a former energy consultant and demands, \u201cWhat energy do you put into your restaurant?\u201d Ragnar confesses he\u2019s never helped out in the kitchen, hosting, etc.</p>, <p>Gordon asks the sickened customers to give him 24 hours to give The Trolley Stop Cafe a serious overhaul and asks them to return the next day. Despite what they\u2019ve just seen, they agree. He tells employees to call their loved ones and tell them they\u2019re pulling an all-nighter.</p>, <p>Gordon asks the employees who they think is the biggest problem. Surprise! Darren suggests Ragnar. But he thinks many of his coworkers are afraid to confront him because, at the end of the day, a paycheck is a paycheck. Ragnar seems unfazed by the hate and genuinely surprised by how unhappy the customers are.</p>, <p>As miserable as everyone seems, they\u2019re willing to do what it takes to save The Trolley Stop Cafe. Time for Gordon\u2019s crew to step in and take over!</p>, <p>First up: the decor. \u201cThis restaurant is like an ugly stepchild,\u201d declares Gordon. The restaurant needs a new, clean look. He then goes into the kitchen to analyze the damage.</p>, <p>The kitchen isn\u2019t cleaned regularly. Obviously. Darren thinks the kitchen hasn\u2019t been cleaned since old management was still running the place. Stoves, ovens, and burners haven\u2019t been cleaned in a shockingly long time.</p>, <p>Gordon opens the fridge and discovers moldy food, including the cheese he was served on his nachos earlier. He is livid that Darren voluntarily served him moldy food.</p>, <p>Gordon dishes out some of said moldy food and instructs Aaron, Ragnar, and Darren to eat it. And they actually do. None of them looked like they enjoyed it at all.</p>, <p>\u201cYou should thank yourselves you haven\u2019t killed anybody,\u201d screams Gordon, throwing rancid meat right at them.</p>, <p>While Gordon\u2019s team and The Trolley Stop Cafe team work together to revamp the restaurant, Gordon pulls Darren aside for a quick cooking lesson. He shows how to make traditional Southern fare \u2013 fried green tomato BLT, fried chicken and waffles, pork chops, etc.</p>, <p>We learn Darren lost his father young and his dad was a criminal. Darren doesn\u2019t want to end up like him. Darren, for his part, takes to the lesson eagerly, admitting that he looks up to Ramsay.</p>, <p>\u201cCan you do this? Do you want it?\u201d Gordon asks Darren.</p>, <p>\u201cI want to be proud of The Trolley. I want to be happy at work again,\u201d says Darren, fighting back tears. Gordon can see that. These two have missed a good hugging opportunity.</p>, <p>The feel-good moment is over, and it\u2019s back to work with 18 hours to spare. Darren steps in to train the kitchen staff on what he\u2019s learned, and Gordon decides it\u2019s time to hone in on Ragnar.</p>, <p>\u201cWhy did you even contemplate leaving the energy business?\u201d Gordon wants to know. Ragnar said he wanted to continue the family legacy. He doesn\u2019t want to let his family down, but he knows he\u2019s in over his head. Now he\u2019s crying.</p>, <p>\u201cIf you want to run a restaurant, you need to work in it,\u201d says Gordon. Ragnar needs to be in the thick of it, day in and day out. He tells Ragnar to \u201clead like a boss.\u201d No hug for these two, either, but Gordon\u2019s words are definitely sinking in with Ragnar.</p>, <p>Back to the renovations we go! Gordon unveils the new kitchen.</p>, <p>A Vitamix! Griddle pans! No grime or grease anywhere! A refrigerator with windows! (I want one!) The kitchen staff is super excited for their shiny new toys.</p>, <p>And all of a sudden, Aaron Sanchez shows up! It turns out Gordon\u2019s Masterchef co-judge lives two blocks from the cafe.</p>, <p>\u201cYou represent our city and food culture,\u201d Aaron informs the staff.</p>, <p>Gordon commands the staff to make everything on the menu for him and Aaron. The food looks decent, with one major faux pas \u2013 someone plated raw fried chicken. With five minutes left to the grand reopening. Not good.</p>, <p>Gordon\u2019s managed to wrangle up a second line outside for the reopening \u2013 the small parade included a trolley, live jazz music, even cheerleaders! Even the cops have reported for duty. Gordon comes out to greet the crowd and introduce them to the new-and-improved cafe.</p>, <p>Patrons are immediately greeted by Ragnar!\xa0They venture farther into the restaurant and see brighter, better decor, with matching tables.\xa0 The bar, meanwhile, has been transformed into a ticket booth.</p>, <p>\u201cI feel like I\u2019m riding in a streetcar,\u201d says one customer.</p>, <p>Retired Saints Player Tracy Porter is there, as is a country singer. Guest appearances everywhere! Everyone\u2019s excited to try out the new eats. The kitchen staff starts making orders immediately.</p>, <p>Ragnar is going around and greeting the guests at each table. He\u2019s a bit awkward, but he\u2019s learning, and he\u2019s making quite the effort.</p>, <p>Moment of truth: What do the guests think of the food? Well, at one table, the chicken and waffles are a bust. The chicken is still coming out undercooked, as is the pork chop. Double whammy: The undercooked meats happen to have arrived at a local food blogger\u2019s table.</p>, <p>Gordon sends the dishes back. Take two on the food: Still a miss with the chicken. Uh-oh. Gordon\u2019s getting mad now, and beckons to Darren to demand what\u2019s going on and to get it together, which he does. The third time\u2019s the charm, and the blogger is pleased and salmonella is avoided.</p>, <p>At the end of the night, customers leave with full, happy bellies, and vow to return. Gordon saves the day! Ragnar shakes Gordon\u2019s hand and thanks him for everything.</p>, <p>\u201cWelcome to our world,\u201d says Gordon. Let\u2019s hope Ragnar sticks with it and brings his energy consultant skills into the restaurant his family has worked so hard to build.</p>, <p>\u201cIf I can get through the last 24 hours, I can get through anything,\u201d says Ragnar. And then Darren and Ragnar hug. They hug!</p>, <p>Three months later, the team checks in. Darren\u2019s still loving his job, Ragnar\u2019s a regular, and Aaron, Darren, and Ragnar are all working together well. Customers are enjoying the new look and delicious food. The South has risen once again!</p>, <p>Gordon Ramsay\u2019s 24 Hours to Hell and Back airs on Wednesdays at 9 p.m. on <a href="https://www.fox.com/">FOX</a>.</p>, <p>\xa9 Copyright 2004 - 2018 Monsters and Critics \xb7 All Rights Reserved \xb7 All logos &amp; trademarks belong to their respective owners\xb7 All images are used with permission or licensed.</p>]
[<p class="tempo-iframe-embed-container"><iframe aspect_ratio="56.347826086957%" class="tempo-iframe-embed" height="324" scrolling="no" src="https://wpcomwidgets.com?width=575&amp;height=324&amp;frameborder=0&amp;style&amp;class&amp;scrolling=no&amp;webkitallowfullscreen&amp;mozallowfullscreen&amp;allowfullscreen&amp;resize=0&amp;replace_attributes=1&amp;fallback=%3Cp+class%3D%22protected-embed-fallback%22%3EThis+embed+is+invalid%3C%2Fp%3E&amp;_data=PGlmcmFtZSBzcmM9Ii8vc2hhcmUuZWxsZW50dWJlLmNvbS92aWRlby9kci1kYXgtc2hlcGFyZC1nZXRzLWEtYmlydGhkYXktc2NhcmUtZXh0ZW5kZWQuaHRtbCIgd2lkdGg9IjU3NSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIzMjQiIGZyYW1lYm9yZGVyPSIwIiBzY3JvbGxpbmc9Im5vIiBhbGxvd2Z1bGxzY3JlZW49IiIgY2xhc3M9IiIgcmVzaXplPSIwIiByZXBsYWNlX2F0dHJpYnV0ZXM9IjEiPjwvaWZyYW1lPg%3D%3D%2Ca429cb420fc0d3c0c29bbc260857758acf123ca0&amp;_tag=protected-iframe&amp;_hash=6c43f10ae3b7176d05b0e212e80ff1e0" width="575"></iframe></p>, <p>It doesn\u2019t get any sweeter than this.</p>, <p>While celebrating his 44th birthday on Thursday\u2019s episode of\xa0<a href="https://people.com/tag/the-ellen-degeneres-show"><i>The Ellen DeGeneres Show</i></a>, <a href="https://people.com/tag/dax-shepard">Dax Shepard</a> was joined by his wife <a href="https://people.com/tag/kristen-bell">Kristen Bell</a>, who asked for the perfect gift idea to give to a wonderful husband on his special day.</p>, <p>During a question-and-answer session, <i>The Good Place</i> star, 38, surprisingly popped up in the audience. And after being playfully asked to state her name, the actress asked her husband, \u201cwhat would you recommend getting someone very special, like a spouse, for their birthday, or how would you spoil them on their birthday?\u201d</p>, <p>\u201cIn the bedroom,\u201d Shepard, who was wearing a pair of overalls covered with photographs of <a href="https://people.com/tag/brad-pitt/">Brad Pitt</a>\u2019s face \u2014 a gift from Degeneres \u2014 teasingly answered.</p>, <p>\u201cLet\u2019s say I have the bedroom covered,\u201d the mother of two replied with a wink.</p>, <p>After the laughter from the crowd quieted down, Shepard shared that his wife had already given him the best birthday gift of all.</p>, <p>\u201cI would say, please, please, please give that person love and support for 11 years. Give them two beautiful baby girls. And you\u2019re good,\u201d he said.</p>, <p>\u201cYou\u2019re crying, too!\u201d Bell replied, tears welling in her eyes.</p>, <p>\u201cYou sit down, young lady,\u201d her husband quickly replied, after which she sweetly added, \u201cI love you.\u201d</p>, <p><strong>RELATED:\xa0<a href="https://people.com/parents/dax-shepard-kristen-bell-rare-photo-daughters-denim/">Dax Shepard and Kristen Bell Share Rare Photo of Their Daughters Delta, 4, and\xa0Lincoln, 5\xbd</a></strong></p>, <p>During the episode, Shepard also revealed that in his experience, having a birthday that falls so close to New Year\u2019s Day is \u201cthe <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Vthesuv0UDM" target="_blank">worst</a>.\u201d</p>, <p>\u201cCouple reasons,\u201d the\xa0<a href="https://armchairexpertpod.com/pods/sean-hayes" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><em>Armchair Expert</em></a>\xa0podcast host explained. \u201cIt\u2019s\xa0traditionally when you go back to school as a kid. It\u2019s like, \u2018Happy birthday! Go to school!\u2019 And then when you get there, there was a big break, So, when they read the happy birthdays over the loud speaker, you\u2019re among like 30 people who had birthdays. Nothing special!\u201d<br/>\n<br/>\n                  He went on to share that even as an adult, the date brings complications.</p>, <p>\u201cWhen I try to have a birthday party, everyone has just quit eating carbs, they\u2019re not drinking. All this goes out the window in a week, but my birthday is in the first week,\u201d he shared. \u201cI can\u2019t get more than six people to attend my birthday party\u2014and I\u2019m on television and they know Kristen will be there. I also think he has gotten funnier over the years!\u201d</p>, <p>She added, \u201cAt first I was attracted to the way he made me feel, and now I\u2019m attracted to the things I learn from him.\u201d</p>, <p>The couple wed in October 2013 and <a href="https://people.com/parents/kristen-bell-dax-shepard-daughter-kindergarten-school-pictures/">share two daughters</a>, Lincoln, 5\xbd, and Delta, 4.</p>, <p class="text-align-center shop-footer-note">\n                    PEOPLE.com may receive compensation when you click through and purchase from links contained on this website.\n                  </p>, <p>If you have opted in for our browser push notifications, and you would like to\n                  opt-out, please refer to the following instructions depending on your device and\n                  browser. [<p>Just months after revealing their rekindled romance on social media following a brief split in March,\xa0<a href="https://people.com/tag/zayn-malik">Zayn Malik</a> and <a href="https://people.com/tag/gigi-hadid">Gigi Hadid</a>\xa0may have called it quits for the second time. <a href="https://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/gigi-hadid-and-zayn-malik-split-again-theyre-done/" target="_blank">Multiple outlets report</a> that the two <a href="https://www.etonline.com/inside-gigi-hadid-and-zayn-maliks-split-for-the-second-time-116524" target="_blank">recently ended things again</a>.</p>, <p>The high-profile couple first started dating in November 2015, but stirred up the first inklings of their split when Malik, 25, didn\u2019t sit in the audience of the\xa0<a href="https://people.com/tag/victorias-secret-fashion-show/">Victoria\u2019s Secret Fashion Show</a>\xa0in November to cheer on Hadid, 23, as he has done in previous years. [<p>Diddy and Cassie Ventura's <a href="https://www.etonline.com/sean-diddy-combs-splits-from-longtime-girlfriend-cassie-111822" target="_blank">breakup last October after more than a decade of dating</a> is taking a not so amicable turn.</p>, <p>The 32-year-old singer recently went public with her relationship with 25-year-old bullfighter and professional trainer Alex Fine, but a source tells ET that Diddy feels betrayed by Cassie after finding out that she allegedly cheated on him with Fine, whom Diddy actually hired for her as a personal trainer, as well as\xa0paid for.</p>, <p>However, according to <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/01/03/diddy-cassie-new-boyfriend-celebrity-trainer/" target="_blank"><em>TMZ</em></a>, who was first to report the news, sources connected to Cassie and Fine insist the two didn't start dating until after she broke up with Diddy.</p>, <p>Prior to the new drama, Cassie and Diddy's breakup appeared friendly\xa0and even had some fans believing they would be getting back together. The two have been romantically linked as far back as 2007, and last January, the father of six even said he was open to having more kids with Cassie during his appearance on <em>The Breakfast Club.</em>\xa0</p>, <p>\u201cWithout a doubt, I love children,\u201d he said. \u201cI could go to eight without a problem. Can\u2019t stop, won\u2019t stop. Whatever is supposed to happen in the future is going to happen, but that\u2019s something that I want.\u201d</p>, <p>\u201cI would only have it with my girl, of course,\u201d he added.</p>, <p>Though by October, a source told ET <a href="https://www.etonline.com/sean-diddy-combs-splits-from-longtime-girlfriend-cassie-111822" target="_blank">that the two had broken up.</a> Although there were rumors that Diddy was dating 26-year-old model Jocelyn Chew, the source said that the 49-year-old mogul actually wasn't dating anyone at the time.\xa0</p>, <p>Despite their breakup, Cassie <a href="https://www.etonline.com/diddy-reunites-with-ex-cassie-as-coroner-calls-for-additional-investigation-into-kim-porters-death" target="_blank">was there for Diddy one month later</a> when his ex, Kim Porter -- whom he dated on and off for several decades and shared three children with -- <a href="https://www.etonline.com/diddys-ex-girlfriend-kim-porter-dead-at-47-113919" target="_blank">died suddenly.</a> Cassie and Diddy were <a href="https://www.eonline.com/news/988438/diddy-and-ex-girlfriend-cassie-reunite-after-kim-porter-s-death" target="_blank">spotted out together in Los Angeles</a>, the singer presumably supporting her ex during an extremely difficult time.</p>, <p>Cassie herself paid tribute to Porter on Instagram\xa0and praised her ex as "the best father" in the process.</p>, <p>\u201cThere are no words,\u201d she wrote alongside a black-and-white photo of Porter. \u201cAn amazing mother to her beautiful family, lit up every room she entered and now the most beautiful angel \ufffd Sending so much love and my condolences to the Porter and Combs family. I love you @quincy, @kingcombs, Jessie, D\u2019Lila, Chance, @princejdc and @diddy. Puff you are already the best father. I know you will be amazing. Love you too.\u201d</p>, <p>As recently as late December, it appeared Diddy was attempting to reconcile with Cassie. The Bad Boy Entertainment founder took to his Instagram Story to share an intimate photo of Cassie smiling in a hot tub -- adding a heart emoji -- which he posted twice.\xa0</p>, <p>But the very next day, Cassie went public with Fine. Cassie shared a photo\xa0of the two kissing, as well as one of Fine posing with her and her mother at a party.\xa0</p>, <p style=" margin:8px 0 0 0; padding:0 4px;"><a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/Br-vWu7nEV5/?utm_source=ig_embed&amp;utm_medium=loading" style=" color:#000; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px; font-style:normal; font-weight:normal; line-height:17px; text-decoration:none; word-wrap:break-word;" target="_blank">I love you Mommy</a></p>, <p style=" color:#c9c8cd; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px; line-height:17px; margin-bottom:0; margin-top:8px; overflow:hidden; padding:8px 0 7px; text-align:center; text-overflow:ellipsis; white-space:nowrap;">A post shared by <a href="https://www.instagram.com/cassie/?utm_source=ig_embed&amp;utm_medium=loading" style=" color:#c9c8cd; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px; font-style:normal; font-weight:normal; line-height:17px;" target="_blank"> Casandra</a> (@cassie) on <time datetime="2018-12-29T17:52:54+00:00" style=" font-family:Arial,sans-serif; font-size:14px; line-height:17px;">Dec 29, 2018 at 9:52am PST</time></p>, <p>Fine is no stranger to the celebrity world. The elite trainer, who has his own personal training program called Alex Fine Performance, has a number of A-list clients including Jennifer Aniston, Kelly Ripa, as well as<em> Riverdale </em>stars KJ Apa and Charles Melton. He also trains professional athletes including NFL stars Odell Beckham Jr. and Reggie Bush.\xa0</p>, <p>"I built my gym on friend referrals. [<p class="entry-meta"><time class="entry-time" datetime="2019-01-03T16:29:15+00:00">3rd January 2019</time> by <span class="entry-author"><a class="entry-author-link" href="https://www.monstersandcritics.com/author/tanya-clark/" rel="author"><span class="entry-author-name">Tanya Clark</span></a></span></p>, <p><a href="https://www.monstersandcritics.com/tag/the-bold-and-the-beautiful/" title="The Bold and the Beautiful">The Bold and the Beautiful</a> is celebrating its 8,000th episode on Friday January 4, 2019 with a sensational, scintillating, and shocking storyline that promises to rock fans to their very cores. How deliciously soapy!</p>, <p>B&amp;B executive producer and head writer Bradley Bell has promised fans a whopper of an episode to mark the show\u2019s incredible milestone. \u201cWe\u2019re grateful that you\u2019ve allowed us into your homes for over 30 years,\u201d he said recently. \u201cThe 8000th episode is classic Bold and Beautiful drama. The story arc centers around an event so profound, it sends shockwaves throughout the lives of the Forresters, Spencers, Avants, Spectras and Logans for years to come.\u201d</p>, <p>Yikes, if that doesn\u2019t send chills down your spine, nothing will!</p>, <p>B&amp;B debuted on March 23, 1987. As a special remembrance, Bell shared with fans eight of his significant storylines from the last 8,000 episodes. Which of these plots was your personal favorite?</p>, <p><strong>1991:</strong> Eric Forrester (John McCook) marries Brooke Logan (Katherine Kelly Lang) in a lavish wedding in the Mojave Desert where they enjoy horseback rides and an awe-inspiring hot air balloon ride. The day climaxes in a luxurious tent where they consummate their marriage.</p>, <p><strong>1998:</strong> Brazen Brooke debuts her lingerie line, Brooke\u2019s Bedroom, on top of a bed on the Forrester Creations runway. Stephanie Forrester (Susan Flannery) can only glare at her rival!</p>, <p><iframe data-lazy-src="https://www.facebook.com/plugins/post.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2FTheBoldandtheBeautiful%2Fposts%2F10157176898469101&amp;width=500" data-rocket-lazyload="fitvidscompatible" frameborder="0" height="669" scrolling="no" src="about:blank" style="border: none; overflow: hidden;" width="500"></iframe><noscript><iframe frameborder="0" height="669" scrolling="no" src="https://www.facebook.com/plugins/post.php?href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2FTheBoldandtheBeautiful%2Fposts%2F10157176898469101&amp;width=500" style="border: none; overflow: hidden;" width="500"></iframe></noscript></p>, <p><strong>2008:</strong> Katie Logan (Heather Tom) is on life support in need of a heart transplant. Her heroic but troubled brother Storm is a match and he sacrifices himself out of love.</p>, <p><strong>2010:</strong> Stephanie Forrester learns that she has cancer and wants to complete her bucket list. Long story short, she comes upon Skid Row and her life is transformed.</p>, <p><strong>2011-2017:</strong> Steffy Forrester\u2019s wedding appearances take center stage. At Lope\u2019s Aspen wedding she takes her rival\u2019s place donning a mini-skirt and boots, yee haw! Next time Steffy pops up in lace gown riding a motorcycle, and finally she zip-lines to the Australian ceremony from atop the Sydney Opera House.</p>, <p><strong>2015-2016:</strong> The Maya Avant (Karla Mosley) transgender storyline is front burner. Rick Forrester (Jacob Young) proposes but after Maya discloses her truth he ends their relationship. In the end they marry and become surrogate parents.</p>, <p><strong>2016:</strong> Quinn Fuller (Rena Sofer) kidnaps Liam Spencer (Scott Clifton) at a remote cabin and convinces him that they are Adam and Eve, husband and wife.</p>, <p><strong>2018:</strong> Dollar Bill Spencer (Don Diamont) is shot from behind, and it\u2019s a life or death situation. But the cops can\u2019t figure out who did it because he has too many enemies!</p>, <p><em>The Bold and the Beautiful airs weekdays during the day on CBS.</em></p>, <p>\xa9 Copyright 2004 - 2018 Monsters and Critics \xb7 All Rights Reserved \xb7 All logos &amp; trademarks belong to their respective owners\xb7 All images are used with permission or licensed.</p>]

[<p>The moment Ben Barnes stepped on screen as Billy Russo in <a href="http://www.gizmodo.com.au/2017/11/netflixs-the-punisher-is-a-brutal-humanisation-of-frank-castle-that-cant-face-its-own-demons">Netflix\u2019s <em>The Punisher</em></a>, comic fans realised that it was only a matter of time before he ended up becoming one of the antihero\u2019s most well-known nemeses, the villain known as Jigsaw.\n</p>, <p>But when we caught up with Barnes during a recent visit to <em>The Punisher</em>\u2019s set during the second season\u2019s filming, he was careful to explain that the path to full-on villainy in his upcoming arc on the show is going to be nuanced, and somewhat different than its comics counterpart. </p>, <p>While Billy\u2019s disfigurement is still a factor in what pushes him to become Jigsaw, <em>The Punisher</em> is much more interested in exploring the fragmented-ness of Billy\u2019s psyche in order to keep the show feeling grounded:</p>, <p>\nAt the end of the first season, we hear the doctors sort of saying that that Ben\u2019s undergone surgery for stab wounds and wounds on his face, so he\u2019s had a plastic surgeon try to fix him. </p>, <p>We\u2019re talking abut a deeply narcissistic character\u2014in season one\u2014whose mask of appeal in terms of doing his hair and the nice suits and all that kind of stuff has been stripped away from him. It\u2019s about what he sees when he looks in the mirror rather than necessarily what other people see, because we didn\u2019t want [Billy\u2019s story] to be a horror show. </p>, <p>It\u2019s something more internal. We don\u2019t refer to the character as Jigsaw in the series, but he very much has a jigsaw puzzle in his brain. It\u2019s not about his face, it\u2019s about the psychological, which is really something we wanted to focus on this season.\n</p>, <p>Though Jigsaw\u2019s very much going to be a major thorn in Frank Castle\u2019s side in the new season, Barnes also insisted that the show is also set to really focus on Jigsaw\u2019s personal predicament as a means of humanising him:</p>, <p>\nIt\u2019s not just about the physical. He\u2019s had his head very much traumatized in the same way that many many veterans have been and he\u2019s trying to deal with that. He\u2019s got brain damage and severe issues with his memory. He\u2019s trying to piece together what happened and who he is, and at one point the metaphor is used that his brain is the jigsaw they\u2019re trying to put back together.\n</p>, <p>With Netflix\u2019s partnership with Marvel <a href="http://www.gizmodo.com.au/2018/12/marvelsdaredevil-writer-i-thought-it-was-too-big-to-fail">seeming all but over with</a>, this is probably going to be <em>The Punisher</em>\u2019s last shot at wowing audiences and figuring out how (if at all) the character should fit into the larger Marvel Cinematic Universe.</p>, <p>From the sounds of it, the show\u2019s creative team knows that now\u2019s the time to shine by getting a little experimental with things, and it\u2019s only a matter of time until we can figure out whether they gambit\u2019s going to pay off. <a href="http://www.gizmodo.com.au/2018/12/heres-your-first-tiny-little-tease-for-the-punisherseason-2">We\u2019re still waiting to hear just when</a> <em>The Punisher</em> season two will drop on Netflix.</p>]

Reilly, Robert Redford and Lin-Manuel Miranda, but Christian Bale and Oliva Coleman may also pull off surprise wins in their categories.</p>, <p>For Best Animated Film we hope the remarkable and charming Isle of Dogs wins, but it might lose out to the very popular Spiderman: Into the Spiderverse.</p>, <p>In Foreign Language film, a category packed with amazing films this year, expect to see the remarkable ROMA take home the award, continuing it\u2019s streak of wins heading into the Oscars.</p>, <p>And in TV we expect \u201cKilling Eve\u201d and \u201cThe Marvelous Ms. Maisel\u201d to take home awards for best drama and comedy respectively.</p>, <p>The evening\u2019s festivities start at 6 p.m. here on KVOA News 4. [<p class="blog-post__byline">\n<time class="publish-date js-publish-date" data-pubdate-value="2019010306" datetime="2019-01-03T06:59:39">January 03, 2019</time>\n<span class="authors">\n6:59am PT\nby\n<span class="js-authors-list">\nAshley Cullins </span>\n</span>\n</p>, <p>On Aug. 13, 2016, Amber Heard was being grilled by Blair Berk, a top Hollywood attorney employed by her now ex-husband Johnny Depp, in a Century City law office. "Johnny and I refer to his other personality, the part of him that is present when he beats me up \u2014 we call that the monster and have called [that] the monster for many years," Heard recounted during a deposition taken amid the divorce. She added, "I was petrified of the monster."</p>, <p>That 471-page deposition transcript is part of a trove of previously unreleased documents obtained by <em>The Hollywood Reporter </em>along with statements from Heard's close friend Raquel Pennington and the Los Angeles Police Department officers who responded after an altercation between the then-married couple at an L.A. penthouse on May 21, 2016. Heard\u2019s friend Tillett Wright, with whom she had been on the phone before it was allegedly thrown at Heard, had called 911.</p>, <p>The testimony sheds new light on the relationship and will be a point of contention in a court battle in the United Kingdom. The tabloid <em>The Sun</em> is defending itself in a defamation lawsuit filed by Depp over an April 2018 <a href="https://www.thesun.co.uk/tvandshowbiz/6159182/jk-rowling-genuinely-happy-johnny-depp-fantastic-beasts/" target="_blank">story </a>headlined "How can J.K. Rowling be \u2018genuinely happy\u2019 casting wife-beater Johnny Depp in the new <em>Fantastic Beasts</em> film?" The article referenced<em> Aquaman</em> star Heard's application for a restraining order against the actor, which centers on that May 2016 night, and said the actress "recounted a detailed history of domestic abuse incidents, some of which had led to her fearing for her life."</p>, <p>The stars have painted conflicting portraits in the press of abuse in their relationship \u2014 even sparking an arbitration proceeding over an allegation that Depp defamed Heard and violated the nondisclosure agreement that was negotiated during their divorce. The actor publicly denied abusing Heard in multiple interviews last fall, and his lawyer Adam Waldman told <em>THR</em> in October that Depp's legal team has evidence that Heard "severely injured" Depp and "faked" abuse allegations. All of which, Heard claims, is false and defamatory.</p>, <p>Heard's account of the events leading up to the split, along with those of other witnesses, will be scrutinized as <em>The Sun</em> defends its story. Heard has asked to testify in the U.K. proceeding, but a source with knowledge of the matter says Depp's legal team has refused to allow it and even threatened to sue her for violating their NDA if she does. That's why Heard's previous divorce testimony could become key, although Depp's camp insists she'll be allowed to testify if <em>The Sun</em> calls her.</p>, <p>There are high stakes in the case, and a different set of legal standards than Hollywood stars are typically used to. In the U.S., the person suing for defamation must prove the statement concerning him or her was false, but in the U.K. the allegedly defamatory statement is generally presumed false unless the defendant can prove it was true. For that reason, testimony about the alleged abuse will play prominently in Depp's U.K. case \u2014 where it is up to <em>The Sun</em> to disprove Depp's claims of what happened that night.</p>, <p>In the deposition transcripts obtained by <em>THR</em>, Heard claimed that on May 21, 2016 at the L.A. residence, Depp threw her phone at her "as hard as he could" and it hit her in the face. She claims he then grabbed her by the hair and she screamed for help. She stated that he "broke a lot of glass things that left glass on the floor," and the ground was covered in damaged objects including silver candlesticks and a lamp, among other items.</p>, <p>That's when, according to the deposition, Heard's friend Raquel Pennington arrived at the penthouse. Pennington testified that she'd been in an adjacent apartment and came over after Heard sent a text asking her to. When she arrived, she heard Depp yelling. Pennington said Heard asked for help and told her Depp had hit her with the phone. She said Depp was "swinging around" a magnum bottle of wine and knocking things off the counter with it. Pennington testified that Depp's yelling eventually prompted his security team to enter, and one of the guards convinced him to leave. She also said that she had taken "dozens of photos" of Heard's bruises during the course of their friendship, including on that night.</p>, <p>The LAPD officers who responded to the 911 call that night also were deposed as part of the divorce proceeding. Officer Melissa Saenz, in a July 18, 2016 deposition, testified that Heard refused to give her name, so she didn't realize who the famous actress was until weeks later. Saenz said Heard was crying but she did not see any marks, bruises, swelling or signs of injury on her face. The officer also testified that she inspected the apartment and saw no signs of shattered glass or broken items. Saenz said Heard repeatedly "shook her head" in response to questions and did not want to talk, and that she had no probable cause to believe a crime had been committed. Officer Tyler Hadden shared similar testimony.</p>, <p>Heard testified that she declined to give a statement to the officers at the advice of her lawyer. Meanwhile, Pennington said the officers saw "all of the damage," including the broken glass, and offered to "go arrest him right now" if Heard filed a report. LAPD officers Saenz and Hadden denied in their depositions ever saying that.</p>, <p>Berk, the lawyer who questioned Heard on behalf of Depp, asked her whether she had ever struck, slapped or thrown an object at the actor. Heard said she "did her best" to defend herself against her bigger, stronger husband.</p>, <p>Depp recounted a different set of events leading up to that evening. The actor, in a July 2018 filing in <em>The Sun</em> defamation lawsuit, claimed Heard was "aggressive and violent" and punched him in the face twice the night of April 21, 2016 after he was late to her birthday dinner. The night of May 21, he said he went to the penthouse to retrieve some of his belongings and brought two of his security guards with him because he "was concerned about what Ms. Heard might do."</p>, <p>Depp said he tossed the phone on the sofa and it didn't hit Heard, nor did he touch her. He claimed Heard started yelling at him after he walked across the room and that's when his security guards came in and she started crying. He also claimed the damage in any photos taken by Pennington that show smashed items in the penthouse and Heard's injured face were not caused by him, and that "hardcopy photographs were put in evidence, but neither the original images nor the associated metadata were produced."</p>, <p>While the depositions may play a role in the U.K. court proceedings, the relationship is also being reexamined as the stars' conflicting accounts continue to make headlines two years after their split.</p>, <p>Depp took his claims public, at length, in a <a href="https://www.gq-magazine.co.uk/article/johnny-depp-interview-2018" target="_blank"><em>British GQ</em> feature</a> published on Oct. 2 with a cover line teased as, "The divorce. The violence. The excess. The vengeance." In response, Heard's reps called Depp's framing of the issue "outrageous" and characterized it as "psychological abuse." Depp's team fired back, teasing evidence to be submitted in the U.K. suit that would show "Ms. Heard repeatedly violently attacked and severely injured Mr. Depp, and then faked abuse allegations against him."</p>, <p>As part of their divorce, the stars agreed not to discuss their marriage or make derogatory statements about each other. In an arbitration demand, Heard claims Depp violated that agreement and defamed her in several media outlets this fall by giving the impression that she falsely claimed to have been physically abused. The actress argues the statements, including ones made by Waldman on Depp's behalf to <em>THR</em>, were made with malice and she\u2019s entitled to punitive damages.</p>, <p>Recently, Heard penned a <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/opinions/ive-seen-how-institutions-protect-men-accused-of-abuse-heres-what-we-can-do/2018/12/18/71fd876a-02ed-11e9-b5df-5d3874f1ac36_story.html?utm_term=.caae2a57a9e5" target="_blank"><em>Washington Post</em> op-ed</a>, titled "I spoke up against sexual violence \u2014 and faced our culture\u2019s wrath. That has to change." Although Depp\u2019s name isn't mentioned, the piece was widely interpreted as being about him. The actress wrote that she "became a public figure representing domestic abuse" and "felt the full force of our culture\u2019s wrath for women who speak out." Heard says she was told she'd be blacklisted, a global fashion brand dropped her as its celebrity face and it was unclear whether her <em>Justice League</em> and <em>Aquaman</em> roles would remain hers. In response, Depp's lawyer Waldman stated that Heard\u2019s column was an "abuse of the #metoo movement" and claimed she "masquerades as victim rather than abuser."</p>, <p>A hearing in the U.K. matter is currently set for Feb 22, and Waldman says Depp's team will introduce evidence including multiple depositions, photographs and eyewitness statements.</p>, <p>In response to Waldman's statements, and Depp's claims in the U.K. filings, Heard's lawyer Eric George tells <em>THR</em>, "Mr. Depp\u2019s ongoing defamation and violation of the parties\u2019 confidentiality agreement is already the subject of a pending arbitration. We won\u2019t dignify his comments with any further response.\u201d</p>, <p>Waldman, meanwhile, claims Heard withdrew her arbitration complaint and suggests that if she "would like to go to court ... we will see her there."</p>, <p>\n<div class="embedded-content" data-amp-enabled="1" data-nid="1166004" data-nodetype="news" data-template="readmore">\n<script type="application/json">\n        {\n          "nid": 1166004,\n          "type": "news",\n          "title": "Amber Heard on Her Secret Passion, Elon Musk and a Splashy New Role",\n          "path": "https://www.hollywoodreporter.com/features/amber-heard-aquaman-elon-musk-dedication-activism-1166004","media": {"width":1500,"height":844,"extension":"jpg","file_size":206742,"mime_type":"image\\/jpeg","type":"image","path":"sites\\/default\\/files\\/2018\\/12\\/thr-photographed_by_ruven_afanador-20181102_thr_amber_heard_s01_203-splash-2018.jpg","orientation":"landscape","id":"1166111","caption":"\\"When you travel ... you can find yourself realizing that, while you\\u2019re never actually alone, you\\u2019ve just gone a month without being around a single person who knows you,\\" says Amber Heard, photographed Nov. 2 at Milk Studios in Los Angeles. [<p>John Ronald Reuel Tolkien, an acclaimed English writer, philologist\xa0and university professor, was born 127 years ago on Jan. 3. He is best known for high fantasy works including \u201cThe Lord of the Rings\u201d and \u201cThe Hobbit.\u201d He died in 1973 and some of his works were posthumously published by his son.</p>, <p>Here are some inspirational quotes from the author, taken from <a href="https://www.brainyquote.com/authors/j_r_r_tolkien" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Brainy Quote</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/quotes/656983.J_R_R_Tolkien?page=4" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Good Read.</a></p>, <p>1. "All that is gold does not glitter, not all those who wander are lost; the old that is strong does not wither, deep roots are not reached by the frost.\u201d</p>, <p>2. \u201cThe world is indeed full of peril, and in it there are many dark places; but still there is much that is fair, and though in all lands love is now mingled with grief, it grows perhaps the greater.\u201d</p>, <p>3. \u201cFantasy is escapist, and that is its glory. If a soldier is imprisoned by the enemy, don't we consider it his duty to escape?. . .If we value the freedom of mind and soul, if we're partisans of liberty, then it's our plain duty to escape, and to take as many people with us as we can!\u201d</p>, <p>4. \u201cThere is nothing like looking, if you want to find something. You certainly usually find something, if you look, but it is not always quite the something you were after.\u201d</p>, <p><blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en"><a href="https://twitter.com/GranthBooks/status/1080741074367401984"></a></blockquote></p>, <p>5. \u201cDarkness\xa0must pass. A new day will come. And when the sun shines, it will shine out the clearer.\u201d</p>, <p>6. \u201cIf more of us valued food and cheer and song above hoarded gold, it would be a merrier world.\u201d</p>, <p>7. \u201cFairy tale does not deny the existence of sorrow and failure: the possibility of these is necessary to the joy of deliverance. It denies (in the face of much evidence, if you will) universal final defeat...giving a fleeting glimpse of Joy; Joy beyond the walls of the world, poignant as grief.\u201d</p>, <p>8. \u201cIt is not our part to master all the tides of the world, but to do what is in us for the succor of those years wherein we are set, uprooting the evil in the fields that we know, so that those who live after may have clean earth to till. What weather they shall have is not ours to rule.\u201d</p>, <p>9. \u201cThere are no safe paths in this part of the world. Remember you are over the Edge of the Wild now, and in for all sorts of fun wherever you go.\u201d</p>, <p>10. \u201cAll your words are but to say: you are a woman, and your part is in the house. But when the men have died in battle and honor, you have leave to be burned in the house, for the men will need it no more. But I am of the House of Erol and not a serving-woman. I can ride and wield blade, and I do not fear either pain or death.\u201d</p>, <p> <span class="figure image" itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject"> <picture class="mapping-embed lazysize" height="3334" itemprop="contentUrl" width="5000"><!--[if IE 9]><video style="display: none;"><![endif]--><source data-srcset="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg 1x" media="(min-width: 1200px)"/><source data-srcset="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed-md/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg 1x" media="(min-width: 992px)"/><source data-srcset="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed-md/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg 1x" media="(min-width: 768px)"/><source data-srcset="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed-md/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg 1x" media="(min-width: 481px)"/><source data-srcset="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed-sm/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg 1x" media="(min-width: 0px)"/><!--[if IE 9]></video><![endif]--><img alt="J.R.R. Tolkien" class="mapping-embed lazysize lazyload" height="3334" itemprop="contentUrl" src="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg" title="" width="5000"/></picture><meta content="https://s1.ibtimes.com/sites/www.ibtimes.com/files/styles/embed/public/2019/01/03/jrr-tolkien.jpg" itemprop="url"/><meta content="5000" itemprop="width"/><meta content="3334" itemprop="height"/> <span class="figcaption"> <span class="caption" itemprop="caption">A copy of 'The Story of Kullervo' by J.R.R. Tolkien is pictured in London, Aug. 25, 2015. </span> <span class="credit" itemprop="copyrightHolder">Photo: JUSTIN TALLIS/AFP/Getty Images</span> </span> </span></p>, <p>\xa0</p>]
[<p class="cm-header-desktop__cta" data-reactid="60">Subscribe Now</p>, <p class="cm-header-desktop__offer" data-reactid="61">Get the Magazine</p>, <p class="cm-header-dropdown__dek" data-reactid="67">1 Year for $15</p>, <p class="dek" data-reactid="150">You know what's fun? Just dropping in on the most deranged show on television.</p>, <p>Let me tell you about one of my favorite traditions: at least twice a year for the last four years, I drop in on <em>Gotham</em>, the Fox drama about the early days of Jim Gordon, future police commissioner in the <em>Batman</em> comics, and the various deranged villains who take over his city on a weekly basis. I&amp;aposm being quite literal here: I don&amp;apost keep up with <em>Gotham</em>. I don&amp;apost watch it week to week, nor do I do a catchup binge. I just swan dive right in, with perfect and beautiful form and probably a snack, and I queue up the last episode that aired, or watch it live if I&amp;aposm feeling dangerous. It&amp;aposs a thrilling way to live. You should try it.</p>, <p><em>Gotham</em> is perhaps the greatest show to drop in on sans context, mostly because it makes about as much sense episode-to-episode as it does year-to-year. What started as a series that was originally pitched as an origin story about cops in a bad city in the years leading up to Batman&amp;aposs arrival\u2014along with the host of theme-party villains he&amp;aposd inspire\u2014has turned into a show that&amp;aposs pretty much Batman without Batman, about all these deranged, horny, and immortal (?) villains that have shown up years early and are extremely committed to stabbing one another. Yeah, Jim Gordon is there but everyone kind of ignores him, and scrawny teen Bruce Wayne is also around acting as a kid vigilante, which never stops being funny.</p>, <p>Turn on a given episode of <em>Gotham</em>\u2014which is streaming all four seasons on Netflix, and kicks off its final season tonight\u2014and you don&amp;apost really know what you might see. Maybe a bodyguard resurrected as a hulking zombie. Maybe a mind control plague is tearing a marriage to shreds. Maybe you&amp;aposll see one of my favorite things, which is someone yelling an answer at the Riddler before he finishes composing a riddle. For a long time I&amp;aposm pretty sure the show had a long-running plot about Penguin&amp;aposs unrequited love for the Riddler. There&amp;aposs not much <em>Gotham</em> won&amp;apost do, except maybe a story about a woman who isn&amp;apost deranged or in a doomed romance. (To its credit, the show did have one of its deranged women take over a portion of the city and declare it a man-free zone, so I guess <em>Gotham</em> is <em>kind of</em> feminist, if you squint some and huff a bit of glue.)</p>, <p>Call it the <em>Riverdale</em> effect: When your baseline for normal is just <em>bananas all the time</em>, it doesn&amp;apost matter what a show decides to do. Being bewildered becomes a feature, not a bug. Of course, <em>Gotham</em> doesn&amp;apost ground itself the way <em>Riverdale</em> does\u2014the latter show is, despite its absurd plots, a standard soap opera with surprisingly stable relationships. All <em>Gotham</em> has as a foundation is that... Bruce Wayne is going to be Batman someday? On the one hand, this is exhausting. On the other, <em>Gotham</em> could probably pull off an episode where a chinchilla runs for mayor and wins thanks to Russian hackers and maybe some hypnosis from <a href="https://www.gq.com/story/bd-wong-jurassic-world-great-leap-profile">B.D. Wong</a>. (B.D. Wong is on this show.)</p>, <p>Of course, there is <em>craft</em> to Gotham\u2014it is probably the most visually distinct network drama on air, with a vision of Gotham City that&amp;aposs a perfect cross between Tim Burton and Joel Schumacher, parody and paean all at once. It&amp;aposs got <em>delicious</em> scene-chewing performances from actors who all seem to be on different shows at the same time, somehow. And it&amp;aposs always going to choose what&amp;aposs fun over what makes sense.</p>, <p>Unfortunately, <em>Gotham</em>&amp;aposs idea of <em>fun</em> involves lots of maiming and falls mostly on the <em>twisted</em> side of things, so it&amp;aposll never be a good <em>binge</em>. But to drop in on? God yes, watch it. Don&amp;apost know what&amp;aposs going? Doesn&amp;apost matter! You shouldn&amp;apost let that get you down, anyway\u2014dropping in on a show in the middle of its run is a great way to watch TV, and we used to do it all the time. You&amp;aposre smart! You can figure it out, trust me. Going backwards is just as fun as going forwards. Take a hint from <em>Gotham</em>, which has never once cared about when things happen.</p>, <p data-reactid="208">Subscribe now and get a FREE weekender bag and the GQ Style Guide.</p>, <p data-reactid="295"><!-- react-text: 296 -->\xa9 <!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 297 -->2019<!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 298 --> Cond\xe9 Nast. [<p class="entry-meta" data-swiftype-index="false">\n<span class="entry-meta__author">\n<span class="u-lc">by</span>\n<a href="/authors/mike-vulpo">Mike Vulpo</a>\n</span>\n\t\n\t|\n\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<span class="entry-meta__time">\n\t\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\n\t\n\t\n\t\n\t\n\t\n\t\t\n\t\tThu., Jan. 3, 2019 11:07 AM\t\n\t\n\t\n\t\t\t</span>\n</p>, <p class="image__credits">Jim Smeal/Jordan Strauss/Invision/AP/REX/Shutterstock</p>, <p>New year, new drama.</p>, <p>It's no secret that <strong><a href="/news/jenelle_evans">Jenelle Evans</a></strong> and <strong>Kailyn Lowry</strong> aren't the best of friends. While they may be on <em>Teen Mom 2</em> together, the pair doesn't exactly see eye to eye on many issues.</p>, <p>With a new season kicking off later this month, some fans may be hoping that 2019 will bring a fresh start for the pair. From the looks of things, it's just not the case.</p>, <p>It all started when Kailyn took to Twitter and confirmed a <a href="https://twitter.com/TheAshleysRR/status/1080595332960903168" target="_blank">report</a> that says crew members are refusing to work on Jenelle's shoots because they're afraid of her husband <strong>David Eason</strong>.</p>, <p>"I will not be attending any type of reunion on the same day or weekend as Jenelle &amp; David for the same reasons," she <a href="https://twitter.com/KailLowry/status/1080646130977947648" target="_blank">wrote</a> on Twitter.</p>, <p><strong><a href="https://www.eonline.com/photos/21284/teen-mom-status-check-which-couples-are-still-together" target="_blank"><em>Teen Mom</em> Status Check: Which Couples Are Still Together?</a></strong></p>, <p>As it turns out, Jenelle may have seen the comments and tried to set the record straight on Instagram Stories.</p>, <p class="image__credits">Instagram </p>, <p>"MTV doesn't even come to my house to film, where David is. I solely film with my mom at lunches or with the kids and my mom. David is never involved," she explained. "This was my contract 'terms' to begin with. Everyone still has to make a huge deal about David when he isn't involved."</p>, <p>Jenelle continued, "My husband DOES NOT interfere with filming. Producers get angry when David is going to be at my child's soccer games, or if I go to LA to do business, etc\u2026.they CHOOSE not to come."</p>, <p>Last year, David <a href="https://www.eonline.com/news/915157/teen-mom-s-jenelle-evans-speaks-out-after-david-eason-s-alleged-homophobic-tweets-surface" target="_blank">was fired</a> from <em>Teen Mom</em> after making headlines for his homophobic tweets. Jenelle would later defend her husband saying he "doesn't hate people from the LGBT community."</p>, <p>Ultimately,\xa0the MTV reality star\xa0wasn't impressed with Kailyn's latest comments today.</p>, <p>"Then you got this dumb c--t tweeting about me again to make herself relevant\u2026all you have to worry about is my babygirl," she shared on Instagram Stories before delivering a guide on how to handle haters. Step one: "Don't let ANYONE bring you down."</p>, <p><em>Teen Mom 2</em> kicks off a brand-new season January 14 at 9 p.m. on MTV.</p>, <p class="rail__text">\n<a class="link--full rail__link" [<p>Change Location</p>, <p>Newscasts &amp; Videos</p>, <p><strong>WATCH: When Jessica Share bought sperm from an anonymous donor, she never imagined that she would fall in love with him years later.</strong></p>, <p>\n<b></b><span></span>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/pages/sponsored-content-on-global-news/"></a>\n</p>, <p>\n<b></b><span></span>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/pages/sponsored-content-on-global-news/"></a>\n</p>, <p>Many families have unique dynamics, but one U.S. mother has a story unlike most.</p>, <p>In 2005, Jessica Share used an anonymous sperm donor to conceive a child with her then-wife. After the birth of their daughter Alice, the couple used the same sperm donor for their second child, born 18 months after their first.</p>, <p><strong>WATCH BELOW: Why a 27-year-old Canadian woman chose to be single and pregnant</strong></p>, <p>But their marriage didn\u2019t last, and now, Share is in a romantic relationship with her children\u2019s biological father \u2014 a man she connected with 11 years after giving birth to Alice.</p>, <p>\u201cIt was insane to meet someone who shares so many similarities with my children,\u201d Share told Global News of meeting her sperm donor, Aaron Long, for the first time.</p>, <p>\u201cAt the same time, he\u2019s not so much a twin to the girls that you\u2019d even notice him if we\u2019d been seated next to one another in the past decade.\u201d</p>, <p>In an article <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/stories-46427960" rel="noopener" target="_blank">published by the BBC</a>, Share explains that she discovered Long was her children\u2019s donor after Alice completed a DNA testing kit.</p>, <p dir="ltr" lang="en">Alice\u2019s sister was born 18 months later, and it became a fun game to pick out characteristics only the girls shared.</p>, <p>They were extraordinarily tall, not average height as the donor claimed to be, had long, thin mouths, small noses, electric eyes and impeccable vocabularies. <a href="https://t.co/vUUctTO9UX">pic.twitter.com/vUUctTO9UX</a></p>, <p>\u2014 BBC Stories (@bbcstories) <a href="https://twitter.com/bbcstories/status/1080787798528065536?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">January 3, 2019</a></p>, <p><script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>, <p>Share and her wife separated a few years after their second daughter was born, and after years of co-parenting, Share said her ex refused to return Alice\u2019s sister following a vacation, and subsequently cut off all contact with both of them.</p>, <p>\u201cAlice spends her days dreaming of the sister she was raised with and who she is afraid she will never see again,\u201d Share wrote in her BBC essay. \u201cWanting to know what her genetic heritage was, Alice requested a DNA testing kit from her grandmother for Christmas when she was 11 years old.\u201d</p>, <p><strong>READ MORE: <a href="https://globalnews.ca/news/4517577/egg-freezing/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Single women aren\u2019t freezing their eggs for health reasons. Some can\u2019t find partners</a></strong></p>, <p>\u201cThe results came back about eight weeks later. I clicked on the DNA Relatives section of the site, not thinking anything would come of it. But the first thing I read was, \u2018Aaron Long: 50%. Father.\u2019 \u2018Bryce Gallo: 25%. Half-brother\u2019 was right behind.\u201d</p>, <p>Share started searching for Long online, and managed to track down a man living in Seattle, WA., who fit the bill. After discovering school portraits of Long on a social media site, Share saw the resemblance in her daughters.</p>, <p dir="ltr" lang="en">Jessica looked for Alice's biological father online, eventually finding an Aaron Long matching the few details she had about the original donor.</p>, <p>When she saw his school photos that he'd posted online there was no doubt \u2013 her daughters made the same stupid face! <a href="https://t.co/k6RElmyU5m">pic.twitter.com/k6RElmyU5m</a></p>, <p>\u2014 BBC Stories (@bbcstories) <a href="https://twitter.com/bbcstories/status/1080787805360611334?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">January 3, 2019</a></p>, <p><script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>, <p>\u201cThere was no doubt. My daughters make that stupid face,\u201d Share wrote.</p>, <p>\u201cI quickly wrote a message to him on the DNA testing site. It read: <em>Hi Aaron, I actually have two daughters who\u2019d match you (my ex has my youngest daughter; she\u2019s not on the DNA testing site). If you\u2019re interested in trading family photos, etc., we\u2019re available.</em>\u201d</p>, <p><strong>WATCH BELOW: Parenting trends for 2019</strong></p>, <p>Long replied to Share, and sent \u201ca 50-page long life history\u201d to her. The mother also reached out to Gallo, Alice\u2019s listed half-brother, who told her that he discovered Madi, a 19-year-old half-sister, and that he knew of six children conceived from Long\u2019s sperm.</p>, <p>Pretty soon, Share, Long, Gallo, Madi and Alice all agreed to meet \u2014 even though Share was initially hesitant about it.</p>, <p>\u201cI tried to find parenting advice about such a thing and discovered there is relatively little,\u201d she told Global News. \u201cMost people who want to meet their unknown biological parents are adults. Very few children do it with their mom directing the whole thing.\u201d</p>, <p dir="ltr" lang="en">A few months later, Bryce and Madi made plans to visit Aaron in Seattle. </p>, <p>Alice was interested to find out whether the siblings and Aaron resembled her, so her and Jessica joined the unusual family reunion. <a href="https://t.co/mkAZtaNoTZ">pic.twitter.com/mkAZtaNoTZ</a></p>, <p>\u2014 BBC Stories (@bbcstories) <a href="https://twitter.com/bbcstories/status/1080787809420673024?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">January 3, 2019</a></p>, <p><script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>, <p>Still, Share took Alice to meet Long and her half-siblings.</p>, <p>\u201cAaron hosted a party to which he invited multiple housemates, friends from elementary school, high school, and college. All of his ex-girlfriends, and their new partners and children, were invited,\u201d Share wrote of the meeting.</p>, <p>\u201cThey would all camp on the roof and celebrate meeting his biological children.\u201d</p>, <p><strong>READ MORE: <a href="https://globalnews.ca/news/4599925/surrogate-regulations-canada-compensation/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Proposed regulations could change how surrogate moms are compensated</a></strong></p>, <p>While Share was dating another man at the time\xa0 \u2014 coincidentally also named Aaron \u2014 after they broke up, Share and Long formed a romantic bond.</p>, <p>\u201cWhen my relationship with old Aaron ended, I found myself wondering if my children\u2019s person could also be my person, and if Seattle was a place for us to land while we figured it out,\u201d she wrote.</p>, <p dir="ltr" lang="en">"I'd gladly take any of our new half-siblings inside, make them lunch, do their laundry and take care of them forever.</p>, <p>DNA has become far more important than it was when I picked a donor from a page. Yet it hasn't replaced the truism that families are built on love, not genes.\u201d <a href="https://t.co/qWzxtYGZb1">pic.twitter.com/qWzxtYGZb1</a></p>, <p>\u2014 BBC Stories (@bbcstories) <a href="https://twitter.com/bbcstories/status/1080787827774894080?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">January 3, 2019</a></p>, <p><script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>, <p>Despite developing feelings for Long, Share said she was concerned about becoming a couple. \u201cIt wasn\u2019t starting a relationship with him that worried me; it was breaking up,\u201d she explained.</p>, <p>\u201cI felt I had no right to break up with him and hence really muddy the relationship my children could have with him for many years. It took some convincing that we could both navigate this like adults if [we broke up] before I was willing to be involved with Aaron.\u201d</p>, <p>From left: Bryce Gallo, Madi, Jessica Share, Alice and Aaron Long</p>, <p>Now, Share and Alice live with Long in his Seattle home. Alice\u2019s half-sister Madi recently moved in with them, too. Long\u2019s aging mother also lives with the newly formed family.</p>, <p><strong>READ MORE: <a href="https://globalnews.ca/news/4647121/sperm-donors-facebook/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">COMMENTARY: Why men are willing to donate sperm \u2014 and are using Facebook to make the arrangements</a></strong></p>, <p>It is estimated that Long has as many as 67 children conceived through sperm donation, and Share said she would welcome them into her life.</p>, <p>From left: Aaron Long, Madi, Alice and Jessica Share</p>, <p>\u201cWe\u2019ve even joined a Girl Scout troop with another of Aaron\u2019s bio-kids who is the age of my youngest daughter and lives about an hour away,\u201d wrote Share.</p>, <p>\u201cIt\u2019s hard to tell if DNA played a role in our relationship. I know that I am attracted to Aaron for all the reasons that seemed wonderful when shopping for him in a sperm donor catalogue years ago.\u201d</p>, <p>Laura.Hensley@globalnews.ca<br/><a class="twitter-follow-button" data-show-count="false" href="https://twitter.com/lolahensley">Follow @lolahensley</a></p>, <p class="article-copyright">\n\t\t\t\xa9\xa02019\xa0Global News, a division of Corus Entertainment Inc.\t\t</p>, <p>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/canada/">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCanada\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n</p>, <p>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/world/">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tWorld\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n</p>, <p>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/canada/">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCanada\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n</p>, <p>\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/canada/">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCanada\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n</p>, <p class="right-more-link">\n<a href="https://globalnews.ca/pages/flyers/" target="_blank"> More Weekly Flyers </a>\n</p>, <p>Want to discuss?
