[<p>In the 90-year history of the <a data-tag="oscars" href="https://variety.com/t/oscars/" id="auto-tag_oscars">Oscars</a>, the <a data-tag="academy-of-motion-picture-arts-and-sciences" href="https://variety.com/t/academy-of-motion-picture-arts-and-sciences/" id="auto-tag_academy-of-motion-picture-arts-and-sciences">Academy of Motion Picture Arts and Sciences</a> has failed to nominate even a single woman in the best director category 85 times. The Academy is not alone. The Hollywood Foreign Press Assn. has excluded women from this category in 69 of its 76 years of awarding Golden Globes, and did not nominate a single woman in 2018. We are squarely mired in another year of #GoldenGlobesSoMale and may be on the brink of yet another year of #OscarsSoMale.</p>, <p>When questioned about their exclusively male choices in years past, spokespeople for these groups have typically noted that the nominations are a reflection, not a cause, of the wildly skewed gender ratios in the mainstream film industry. This response is only partially accurate.</p>, <p>While women do remain underemployed, accounting for just 11% of all directors working on the 250 top grossing films of 2017, and 18% of those working on the 500 top films, according to the latest\xa0Celluloid Ceiling\xa0report by the Center for the Study of Women in Television and Film, the fact is that awards season provides an avalanche of intense publicity for the nominees. If organizations such as the HFPA and the Academy fail to nominate the worthy contributions of women, their choices add to the suppression of women\u2019s visibility within and outside the industry.</p>, <p> <div class="admz" id="adm-inline-article-ad-1">\n<div class="adma google-publisher" data-device="Desktop" data-width="300">\n<div class="pmc-adm-goog-pub-div ad-text">\n<div class="ad-rotatable adw-300 adh-250" id="gpt-variety-article-mid-article-uid0"></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<section class="c-related c-related--post">\n<h3 class="c-heading c-heading--related">Related</h3>\n<article class="c-card c-card--focus-featured" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">\n<figure class="c-card__image" itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject" style="background-image:url('https://pmcvariety.files.wordpress.com/2018/12/Vice-Behind-The-Scenes.jpg?w=700&amp;h=393&amp;crop=1');">\n<a class="c-card__video-link" href="https://variety.com/video/adam-mckay-heart-attack-vice-christian-bale/">\n<img alt="Adam McKay On How Christian Bale" itemprop="contentUrl" src="https://pmcvariety.files.wordpress.com/2018/12/Vice-Behind-The-Scenes.jpg?w=700&amp;h=393&amp;crop=1"/>\n</a>\n</figure>\n<header class="c-card__header">\n<h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="headline">\n<a href="https://variety.com/video/adam-mckay-heart-attack-vice-christian-bale/">Adam McKay Explains How Christian Bale's Method Acting Helped Him Survive a Heart Attack</a>\n</h3>\n</header>\n</article>\n<article class="c-card c-card--focus-featured" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">\n<header class="c-card__header">\n<h3 class="c-card__title" itemprop="headline">\n<a href="https://variety.com/2019/artisans/production/vice-editor-hank-corwin-1203097877/">'Vice' Editor on Why It Was 'One of the Toughest Movies' He's Ever Worked on</a>\n</h3>\n</header>\n</article>\n</section>\n</p>, <p>In the coming weeks, the entertainment trades and popular press will highlight the accomplishments of the nominees, transforming established directors into brand names and new directors into bankable commodities. Reporters will talk at length about the helmers\u2019 filmographies, determination to realize a vision and mastery of filmmaking techniques.</p>, <p>When film writers detail a director\u2019s filmography, they connect the dots in the nominee\u2019s films, identifying themes and stylistic preferences. This year, we will hear about how <a data-tag="adam-mckay" href="https://variety.com/t/adam-mckay/" id="auto-tag_adam-mckay">Adam McKay</a>\u2019s films, such as\xa0\u201cThe Big Short\u201d\xa0and\xa0\u201cVice,\u201d\xa0focus on master manipulators of largely invisible systems of influence and power. Because <a data-tag="karyn-kusama" href="https://variety.com/t/karyn-kusama/" id="auto-tag_karyn-kusama">Karyn Kusama</a> was overlooked by the HFPA, we are less likely to hear about her command of the thriller and horror genres in films such as\xa0\u201cJennifer\u2019s Body,\u201d\xa0\u201cThe Invitation\u201d and\xa0\u201cDestroyer.\u201d</p>, <p>Reporters will also effuse about a director\u2019s resolve, recounting the unexpected challenges that were overcome in making the film. This year, we will hear about how Alfonso Cuar\xf3n\u2019s\xa0\u201cRoma\u201d\xa0came to be regarded as one of 2018\u2019s best films, despite its cast of unknown actors and use of black-and-white photography. Because <a data-tag="lynne-ramsay" href="https://variety.com/t/lynne-ramsay/" id="auto-tag_lynne-ramsay">Lynne Ramsay</a> was not nominated for a Golden Globe, we are less likely to hear how she juggled Joaquin Phoenix\u2019s busy schedule and a looming premiere date at Cannes when shooting her tense thriller,\xa0\u201cYou Were Never Really Here,\u201d in just eight short weeks.</p>, <p>Finally, media accounts will elaborate on a nominated director\u2019s mastery of filmmaking techniques, discussing the wisdom and elegance of the choice of lenses, lighting, shots and camera movements. We will read about how <a data-tag="damien-chazelle" href="https://variety.com/t/damien-chazelle/" id="auto-tag_damien-chazelle">Damien Chazelle</a> captured the look of NASA footage from the 1960s in\xa0\u201cFirst Man,\u201d\xa0but are less likely to learn how Chlo\xe9 Zhao created the naturalistic style achieved in\xa0\u201cThe Rider,\u201d the devastating tale of how a rodeo cowboy copes with life after suffering a head injury.</p>, <p> <div class="admz" id="adm-inline-article-ad-2">\n<div class="adma google-publisher" data-device="Desktop" data-width="300">\n<div class="pmc-adm-goog-pub-div ad-text">\n<div class="ad-rotatable adw-300 adh-250" id="gpt-dsk-tab-mid-article2-uid1"></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</p>, <p>We don\u2019t notice every awards slight and snub of a deserving director who happens to be female, at least in part because the history of these awards has socialized us to assume that great directors come in only one sex. The awards promote and maintain the make-believe meritocracy that is Hollywood.</p>, <p>Recently,\xa0New York Times\xa0film critic Manohla Dargis mused, \u201cMaybe it\u2019s time for women to burn down the old movie industry, then build a new one.\u201d Part of that reinvention would include a close examination of the mythmaking machinery that has installed men at the top of the directing hierarchy for decades. Just as many film festivals are now reevaluating the gender makeup of their selection committees and criteria, it makes sense for award-granting organizations to undergo a similar reassessment. Another part of the reconfiguration would involve calling out these institutions when they continually fail to recognize women\u2019s worthy contributions, as Natalie Portman did at last year\u2019s Globes when she pointedly noted the \u201call-male nominees\u201d in the directing category. It\u2019s time to recognize that being left out of the nominations means undercutting women\u2019s visibility as film directors, and ultimately short-changing their careers.<span class="Apple-converted-space">\xa0</span></p>, <p><em>Dr. Martha M. Lauzen is the executive director of the Center for the Study of Women in Television and Film and a professor at San Diego State University.</em></p>, <p>In December 1900, authorities investigating a darkened lighthouse off Scotland\u2019s west coast found all three men employed there missing, with no sign of struggle or any other explanation emerging. [<p class="dek margin-16-tb padded-mobile">\n              The engaged couple were joined by McPhee's mom and sister on their island getaway\n            </p>, <p class="dek margin-16-tb padded-mobile">\n                  The engaged couple were joined by McPhee's mom and sister on their island getaway\n                </p>, <p>Aloha! Katharine McPhee and fiance David Foster are living their best life on a vacation to Lanai, Hawaii. Foster, 69, and McPhee, 34, got engaged during the summer of 2018, and have been traveling around the island together, going snorkeling, driving around in a vintage blue car and soaking up the tropical sun.</p>, <p>In a selfie snapped by Foster, McPhee sticks out her tongue next to her husband-to-be, who is sporting a festive tropical shirt. \u201cIsland life,\u201d he captioned the photo.\xa0</p>, <p>\u201cWe genuinely love and respect each other and have for a very long time,\u201d McPhee <a href="https://people.com/music/katharine-mcphee-david-foster-open-up-about-their-love/">told PEOPLE in September</a>. The pair, who have a 34-year age difference, first met in 2006 when\xa0<a href="https://people.com/music/david-foster-jokes-bragging-katharine-mcphee-american-idol/">Foster mentored her</a>\xa0and other contestants on\xa0<a href="https://people.com/music/katharine-mcphee-admits-she-didnt-know-who-david-foster-was-before-she-first-met-him/">Season 5 of\xa0<em>American Idol</em></a>.</p>, <p>Two days after Christmas, McPhee posted a photo of herself sporting a yellow bikini and a flower in her hair, \u201cmele kalikimaka is hawaii\u2019s way\u2026\u201d she captioned the shot, referring to the way to say \u201cMerry Christmas\u201d in Hawaiian. Foster\u2019s daughter Erin, 36, <a href="https://people.com/style/erin-foster-comments-stepmom-katharine-mcphee-bikini-photo/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">teased her soon-to-be step mom</a> in the comments of the photo, writing \u201cGrandma!!!! Wtf I don\u2019t want to be next to you at the pool.\u201d</p>, <p>To kick off the new year, McPhee shared a photo of herself posing in a blue car while wearing a black high-waisted two-piece swimsuit. \u201criding into 2019,\u201d she wrote.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>McPhee channeled her inner Kardashian as she posed for a photo inside of a cabana. The <em>Waitress</em> star\u2019s mom Peisha joined the couple on their trip, and was responsible for taking this sexy snapshot. \u201cif you listen closely, you can actually hear my mom whispering \u201cyou\u2019re doing amazing sweetie!\u201d McPhee wrote, referring to Kris Jenner\u2019s iconic complement.</p>, <p>During thier vacation, McPhee and Foster, as well as McPhee\u2019s mom and sister, Adriana, stayed at the luxurious Four Seasons Resort in Lanai.</p>, <p>McPhee stood by a lounge chair with the ocean as her backdrop as she threw up a peace sign in another vacation snap.</p>, <p>McPhee and her sister prepped for their snorkeling adventure by sporting flippers and masks before diving into the Pacific. \u201cMy little Mermaids!!,\u201d Peisha wrote beside the photo. \u201cGetting ready for our snorkeling trip!\u201d</p>, <p>During the excursion, the former <em>American Idol</em>\xa0contestant wore flippers before hopping in the water to go snorkeling. \u201cI\u2019m coming for you Ariel,\u201d she captioned a boomerang of herself kicking her legs on the boat.</p>, <p>Of course, McPhee couldn\u2019t resist performing a little during their getaway, so she took the stage to sing a rendition of \u201cThat\u2019s Life\u201d from her show <em>Smash.</em>\xa0\u201cHappy New Year!! What entertainment we had !!\u201d her mom captioned a video of McPhee singing.</p>, <p>McPhee and her family enjoyed dinner at the resort while wearing tropical dresses and leis. \u201cAm I not the luckiest and most blessed Mama to have these two beautiful daughters!\u201d Peisha wrote, followed by the hashtags #happiness and #joyful.</p>, <p>Foster posed with his soon-to-be in-laws for a quick photo during a traditional Hawaiian luau. \u201cAMAZING time in Lanai,\u201d Peisha wrote of the snap.\xa0</p>, <p>McPhee and Foster\u2019s relationship began \u201con a friend basis\u201d she told PEOPLE. But it later transformed into a romance that took them both by surprise. \u201cThere are just a lot of things when you look at the history of our relationship, neither of us could have written it. I would never have imagined that this would be our future together,\u201d she says.</p>, <p>The women stopped for a selfie ahead of the luau, with Peisha writing, \u201cHeaven in Lanai with my girls !\u201d</p>, <p>Foster\u2019s daughters, Sara, 37, and Erin, 36, also joined in on the family fun, and Sara posted a cheeky photo with her <a href="https://people.com/style/sara-foster-teases-katharine-mcphee-bikini-instagram/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">soon-to-be stepmom</a>. \u201cWhen your mom refuses to dress age appropriately,\u201d she joked in the caption.</p>, <p>Sara also shared a sweet image of her daughter, Josephine Lena, 3, wearing goggles and a swimsuit that matched hers. \u201cWho wore it better?\u201d she wrote.\xa0</p>, <p>Erin spent some time on the sand in Lanai, and posted a photo of herself sporting a black bikini with the caption: \u201cThought I\u2019d end the year showing a different side of me.\u201d</p>, <p>Erin\u2019s beau Simon Tikhman also joined the vacation. [<p><img alt="*" height="1" src="https://sb.scorecardresearch.com/p?c1=2&amp;c2=6035737&amp;cv=2.0&amp;cj=1" width="1"/></p>, <p>You, the complete first season, is available to stream and download on <a href="http://tidd.ly/f6d3679d" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Netflix</a> now. The brand new thriller series stars Gossip Girl\u2019s Penn Badgley and Once Upon a Time star Elizabeth Lail. The series is based on the book of the same name by Caroline Kepnes and was adapted for TV by Greg Berlanti and Sera Gamble. The series stays largely true to the book throughout the show apart from the ending but why?</p>, <p></p>, <p><em><strong>WARNING: This article contains spoilers about You season 1</strong></em></p>, <p>You ended on a major cliffhanger ending which shocked fans across the globe.</p>, <p>Like in the book, <a href="/showbiz/tv-radio/1066917/You-season-2-spoilers-Netflix-is-Beck-really-dead-Joe-Elizabeth-Lail" target="_blank">Beck (played by Elizabeth Lail) was killed by Joe</a> (Penn Badgley) but the ending also had a shocking twist that diverted drastically from the plot of the novel.</p>, <p>Candace (Ambyr Childers) turned out to be alive and in the final seconds of the finale turned up at Mooney\u2019s bookstore where Joe works.</p>, <p>She said to Joe: \u201cI think we have some unfinished business to talk about\u201d before the screen fades to black.\u201c</p>, <p>In the book, Candace was killed by Joe on Brighton Beach in Brooklyn after she ended their relationship.</p>, <p>From Joe\u2019s perspective, Kepnes writes: \u201cIt wasn't my fault that Candace followed me down to the water's edge and it wasn't my fault that I picked her up and held her down in the water and watched her pass on to the great beyond.</p>, <p>\u201cShe wanted to be there, or she wouldn't have gone down there with me.\u201c</p>, <p></p>, <p><a href="/showbiz/tv-radio/1066340/You-Netflix-spoilers-how-did-Candace-really-die-original-book-plot-Ambyr-Childers" target="_blank"><strong>HOW DID CANDACE REALLY DIE?\xa0</strong></a></p>, <p class="withoutCaption"><img alt="Candace is alive in You on Netflix" class="swap" data-h="350" data-imgcount="1" data-media1="" data-src1="https://cdn.images.express.co.uk/img/dynamic/20/590x/secondary/1671366.jpg?r=1546555878690" data-w="590" src="https://cdn.images.express.co.uk/img/page/preloaderbig.gif" title="Candace is alive in You on Netflix"/></p>, <p>In the TV adaption, Candace cheated on Joe with Elijah (Esteban Benito) and she is assumed to be dead.</p>, <p>Viewers were shocked to see Candace turn up alive, especially fans of the book who know the girl who walks into the bookstore is not Candace.</p>, <p>At the end of the book You, a girl named Amy Adams enters Mooney\u2019s and Joe finds himself immediately falling for her, implying the same story will start all over again with a new victim.</p>, <p>Speaking to the Hollywood Reporter, showrunner Sera Gamble discussed why the finale diverted from the plot of the book and the fate of Candace was different.</p>, <p>She explained: \u201cWe knew we were going to start flashing back to Candace as Caroline does in the book.</p>, <p>\u201cWe started by talking about how people would presume that he has killed her and be increasingly convinced that he had done so the more that they know about Joe throughout the season.</p>, <p>\u201cSo we just wanted to do something more surprising and realize that she was such a substantial and interesting character.</p>, <p>\u201cIt did make the casting process more intense because usually you're not so far into a season and casting someone that you potentially need for later. So we knew that we needed somebody really great and luckily, I had already worked with Ambyr Childers.</p>, <p>\u201cShe was a series regular on Aquarius and I was really familiar with her ability to embody a lot of contradictions in one character.</p>, <p>\u201cI was able to say, \u2018You know, this is an actress I think we can bring in and see a little bit of and then know she'll be able to really sink her teeth into bigger stuff later.\u2019\u201d</p>, <p></p>, <p><a href="/showbiz/tv-radio/1064881/You-season-2-Candace-dead-alive-Ambyr-Childers-Joe-Goldberg-series-spoilers" target="_blank"><strong>IS CANDACE REALLY DEAD?</strong></a></p>, <p class="withoutCaption"><img alt="Candace is alive in You on Netflix" class="swap" data-h="350" data-imgcount="1" data-media1="" src="https://cdn.images.express.co.uk/img/page/preloaderbig.gif" title="Candace is alive in You on Netflix"/></p>, <p>Throughout the series, viewers are largely led to believe Candace is dead and Joe killed her, hence why he keeps having flashbacks to their relationship.</p>, <p>Suspicions grew stronger when Candace\u2019s friend Maddie (Manini Gupta) told Beck people\xa0believe\xa0Joe killed her and she doubted Candace moved to Italy.</p>, <p>Even when Joe showed Beck Candace\u2019s Instagram profile and explained that she changed her name when she moved, it is hard to believe Joe did not kill her as this was not the first time he had been posting from a deceased person\u2019s social media account.</p>, <p>Gamble told Entertainment Weekly that the Candace twist was not planned from the beginning and it was not until episode six that executive producer Greg Berate suggested changing the ending.</p>, <p>She said: \u201cHe\u2019s the one who pinpointed what the most amazing cliffhanger would be that also would allow us to streamline some of the storytelling about the \u201cother women\u201d in Joe\u2019s story.</p>, <p>\u201cSo by the time we were in episode six, when we were [<p>A Dark Knight, the Caped Crusader, ol\u2019 Boogaloo Bats. There is a Batman for all seasons. But whatever you call him, he\u2019s known far and wide as a comic book hero who\u2019s managed to keep relevant in entertainment for decades, re-invented time and time again to answer a nation\u2019s distress Bat-signal all. It was camp colors and <em>biff</em>\u2013<em>bang</em>\u2013<em>pow</em> for the 1960s (the <em>Batman</em> TV show). The darkened days of the\u201980s called for blockbuster art deco madness (Tim Burton\u2019s <em>Batman</em>). The world of the 2000s demanded realism and it got Christopher Nolan\u2019s <em>The Dark Knight</em> trilogy.</p>, <p>These days Batman\u2019s paling around with some superhero friends (<em>Justice League</em>), or growing up so fast in live-action shows like <em>Gotham</em>, which is returning for Season 5 on Thursday. It\u2019s going to be the final season for the FOX show and will at long last complete lil\u2019 Wayne\u2019s transformation into Batman.</p>, <p>Holy review aggregates! That means it\u2019s time to rank everything we got on Batman movies and TV shows by Tomatometer! [<p>Another day, another person being lied to on MTV's <em>Catfish. </em>This week's episode featured Dallas, who was chatting for a while with a woman named Safari. Even though they were supposedly in the same city and super into each other, she kept avoiding meeting up with him and wouldn't video chat because her front-facing camera was broken. Yep, we've heard this story before, which means things predictably didn't end in <em>anyone</em>'s favor. But <a class="E" href="https://www.4search.com/bustle.com/where-are-nae-thomas-from-catfish-now-all-his-secrets-came-out-when-nev-max-came-to-town/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">where are Safari and Dallas from <em>Catfish </em>now</a>, post-episode? </p>, <p>Well... they're definitely not together. As revealed in the episode, Safari wasn't actually who Dallas was talking to. Safari's friend William is the true culprit behind the Catfish, and as Dallas isn't interested in men, it didn't go all that well. </p>, <p>"We were on social media drunk, and [Safari]'s like, 'You should totally DM him,'" William said of how the whole thing started. He was nervous, and wanted to put Dallas at ease in a way he thought only a woman could, so he used Safari's photos and identity to work his way into a conversation with him. His ultimate goal was to perhaps be a part of a threesome or other sexual encounter with Dallas that he might set up while posing as a woman... not exactly an honest start to any kind of relationship.</p>, <p>"Most of his fans are gay," William claimed of Dallas' modeling career. But Dallas retorted that wasn't really relevant, saying who follows him has "nothing to do" with what he likes. Nev thought William was shifting the blame away from himself for lying and almost acting like Dallas was asking for it, but William said he wasn't acting maliciously and that he didn't ask for money, and therefore didn't think he was doing any "harm" by lying. William also argued that the way Dallas poses and the photos he shares "target the gay community" and that he shouldn't make money off of those people if he's not actually gay.</p>, <p>Nev conceded that perhaps his social media presence might give the vibe of someone who may be into guys, but that still doesn't mean it's OK to lie and deceive someone. A straight-up conversation at the start about whether Dallas would be interested in William would have saved everyone a lot of trouble.</p>, <p>When Dallas, Nev, and co. eventually met Safari, she and William stuck with that argument. The two seem to think that just because Dallas has a large gay fanbase, it means he should be open to same-sex partners. But not everyone was having it. "I don't agree with you guys when it comes to [the idea that] because Dallas caters to homosexual fan base, it puts some of the responsibility [on him]," Nev said. His co-host, Tallulah, added that though she can understand the thought process behind their points, it's not their place to force a same-sex encounter onto Dallas by tricking him into thinking he's talking to a woman.</p>, <p>All in all, everyone seemed to agree to disagree about what went down. William apologized, and Dallas said he's not one to hold a grudge. At the two-month check-in, they appeared to still feel that way, and said they haven't talked since filming wrapped.</p>, <p><a class="E" href="https://www.instagram.com/flashman.wade/?hl=en" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Dallas' Instagram feed</a> (which is <em>super </em>NSFW!) doesn't show any signs of William, Safari, or any other romantic partner, <a class="E" href="https://twitter.com/Flashmanwade?lang=en" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">nor does his Twitter</a>. William's last name was never revealed, and he couldn't be easily detected on social media when searched in relation to <em>Catfish. </em>Safari, meanwhile, is <a class="E" href="https://www.instagram.com/theonlysafarii/?hl=en" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">still very active on Instagram</a> (and also has a very NSFW feed), but there's no sign of Dallas there, either, so it's safe to assume they all went their separate ways. Hopefully everyone's moved on to more honest relationships.</p>]
[<p data-reactid="117"><em data-reactid="118">In this op-ed, entertainment news editor Claire Dodson unpacks the news that Ariana Grande is only Coachella's fourth female headliner in the festival's nearly 20-year history.</em></p>, <p data-reactid="119"><a data-reactid="120" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/ariana-grande">Ariana Grande</a><!-- react-text: 121 --> is officially headlining Coachella 2019, which is exciting news for Arianators and the hundreds of millions of people who have streamed <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="122" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/ariana-grande-thank-u-next-justin-bieber-favorite-song">"Thank u, next"</a><!-- react-text: 123 --> since it came out in November. In addition to being the youngest artist ever to headline the music festival, she's also only the <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="124" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/fans-brought-back-jonas-brothers-hannah-montana-headliner-meme-coachella-2019">fourth female artist</a><!-- react-text: 125 --> to nab the much-coveted slot. And that number should stick out not necessarily as <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="126" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/new-study-reports-hollywood-diversity-numbers-have-barely-changed-in-a-decade">great progress</a><!-- react-text: 127 -->, but as a sign of a continued, systemic failure on the part of Coachella, as well as major music festivals around the country, to spotlight women artists with major careers worthy of a headlining spot.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="128"><!-- react-text: 129 -->Prior to Ariana, just three other solo women have headlined the Indio, California, music festival: Bj\xf6rk (who headlined twice), <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="130" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/lady-gaga">Lady Gaga</a><!-- react-text: 131 -->, and <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="132" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/beyonce">Beyonc\xe9</a><!-- react-text: 133 -->. That's <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="134">three</em><!-- react-text: 135 --> in the festival's nearly 20-year history. (English band Portishead, which was given headline status on some 2008 posters, features female singer Beth Gibbons along with other male members of the band.)<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="136"><!-- react-text: 137 -->For context, here's a list of headliners since 1999: Beck, Tool, Rage Against the Machine, Jane\u2019s Addiction, Bj\xf6rk, Oasis, Beastie Boys, Red Hot Chili Peppers, Radiohead, the Cure, Coldplay, Nine Inch Nails, Depeche Mode, Tool again, Bj\xf6rk again, Red Hot Chili Peppers again, Rage Against the Machine again, Prince, Roger Waters, Jack Johnson, Portishead, Paul McCartney, the Killers, the Cure again, Jay-Z, Muse, Gorillaz, Kings of Leon, Arcade Fire, Kanye West, the Strokes, the Black Keys, Radiohead again, Dr. Dre &amp; Snoop Dogg, Blur, the Stone Roses, Phoenix, Red Hot Chili Peppers <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="138">again</em><!-- react-text: 139 -->, OutKast, Muse again, Arcade Fire again, AC/DC, Jack White, Drake, LCD Soundsystem, Guns N\u2019 Roses, Calvin Harris, Radiohead <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="140">again</em><!-- react-text: 141 -->, Beyonc\xe9, and Kendrick Lamar.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="142">Wow, that is a lot of men (and a lot of them white men).</p>, <p data-reactid="143"><!-- react-text: 144 -->Ariana's now-headliner status throws into relief the ridiculously low numbers of women headliners, but people have been pointing out this problem with Coachella specifically, as well as other festivals, for years. In 2013, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="145" href="https://www.buzzfeed.com/verymuchso/where-are-all-the-women-at-coachella?sort=posted&amp;z=3DNF36#.emZxdEa2W"><em data-reactid="146">BuzzFeed</em><!-- react-text: 147 --> found<!-- /react-text --></a><!-- react-text: 148 --> that since Coachella's inception, female-led acts have made up, on average, 16% of a given lineup. As <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="149" href="https://www.refinery29.com/en-us/2015/04/85533/coachella-female-performers-gender-problem"><em data-reactid="150">Refinery29</em><!-- react-text: 151 --> pointed out<!-- /react-text --></a><!-- react-text: 152 --> in 2015, the hashtag "#brochella" exists for a reason.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="153"><!-- react-text: 154 -->In 2018, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="155" href="https://pitchfork.com/features/festival-report/tracking-the-gender-balance-of-this-years-music-festival-lineups/"><em data-reactid="156">Pitchfork</em><!-- react-text: 157 --> tracked the lineups<!-- /react-text --></a><!-- react-text: 158 --> of major music festivals that year in the U.S. and charted the genders of the top 10 acts billed for each one. Seven out of 10 were marked as male for Coachella; for Bonnaroo and Boston Calling, the number was nine out of 10; for Lollapalooza and Sasquatch, it was 10 out of 10 for male acts. <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="159">Pitchfork</em><!-- react-text: 160 -->'s own festival that year was more equal, with six male acts, one mixed group, and three female acts.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="161"><!-- react-text: 162 -->The numbers are largely bad all around, even considering that last year 45 festivals around the world <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="163" href="https://pitchfork.com/news/30-music-festivals-pledge-gender-equal-lineups-by-2022/">pledged gender parity</a><!-- react-text: 164 --> in their lineups by 2022. That's only three years away, but clearly, there's still monumental work to be done. Notably, Coachella <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="165" href="https://www.altpress.com/news/festivals_pledge_for_gender_balanced_lineups_by_2022_prs_foundation/">is not</a><!-- react-text: 166 --> one of the 45.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="167"><!-- react-text: 168 -->The reason why this happens is, well, sexism. But the "why" permeates a historically <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="169" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2018/01/25/arts/music/music-industry-gender-study-women-artists-producers.html">male-dominated music industry</a><!-- react-text: 170 -->, in which men are still wield a lot of power all the way down the chain, including festival organizers, bookers, label reps, producers, sound engineers, and so forth. Take three of the biggest music festivals in the U.S., for example: Coachella, Bonnaroo, and Lollapalooza. All three were founded by men \u2014 Paul Tollett and Rick Van Santen (Coachella), Ashley Capps and the male-led team of Superfly Productions (Bonnaroo), and Jane's Addiction singer Perry Farrell (Lollapalooza).<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="171"><!-- react-text: 172 -->And then there are the artists: Women artists, especially in genres like <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="173" href="https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/rock/8220767/women-alternative-rock-radio-alice-merton-kflay-st-vincent">alternative rock</a><!-- react-text: 174 --> and country, just aren't given <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="175" href="https://variety.com/2018/music/news/country-music-women-nashville-radio-fewer-slots-1202977051/">as much radio play</a><!-- react-text: 176 -->, which could mean lower Billboard chart numbers, which could mean more rationalizations from festival bookers about why they're booking so many more male acts. All that is not even to mention the festival atmosphere itself, in which women are especially at risk <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="177" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/sexual-harassment-was-rampant-at-coachella-2018">for rampant sexual harassment</a><!-- react-text: 178 -->.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="179">There's a lot going on in the music industry right now, as it struggles to right the embedded gender imbalances that have existed for far too long. And it will obviously take a lot of work, from a variety of different people in power, to get to a stage where all festival lineups are completely equal and where men aren't the defining voices on radio and streaming charts.</p>, <p data-reactid="180"><!-- react-text: 181 -->Meanwhile, history is already looking back on those 20 years of missed opportunities for women and nonbinary musicians at Coachella. Ariana is a woman with No. 1 singles and is clearly an international pop force. But you know some other female singers with No. 1s? Mariah Carey, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="182" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/rihanna">Rihanna</a><!-- react-text: 183 -->, Janet Jackson, Madonna, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="184" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/kelly-clarkson">Kelly Clarkson</a><!-- react-text: 185 -->, Katy Perry, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="186" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/cardi-b">Cardi B</a><!-- react-text: 187 -->, Jennifer Lopez, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="188" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/taylor-swift">Taylor Swift</a><!-- react-text: 189 -->, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="190" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/tag/alicia-keys">Alicia Keys</a><!-- react-text: 191 -->.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="192"><!-- react-text: 193 -->Sure, not all of those women will be available or willing to do festivals in a given year \u2014 but in the 2010s, 47% of No. 1 songs have so far been performed by women as of 2017, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="194" href="https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/7616906/leading-ladies-women-success-hot-100-chart"><!-- react-text: 195 -->according to <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="196">Billboard</em></a><!-- react-text: 197 -->. That's a major chunk of artists who are not making it into major festival headlining spots.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="198"><!-- react-text: 199 -->There's no valid excuse for the current level of inequality in festival booking and there's <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="200">never</em><!-- react-text: 201 --> been one. In December, Ariana herself talked about just this topic. "I would just love to see a chart with as many women on top as men,\u201d <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="202" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/ariana-grande-called-out-music-industry-sexism-billboard-interview">Ariana said then</a><!-- react-text: 203 -->. \u201cIt\u2019s just so male-dominated. It\u2019s so easy for them. There are so many unbelievable female artists out there that try so much harder."<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="204">And, really, who needs to see Radiohead headline a festival for the millionth time?</p>, <p data-reactid="205"><strong data-reactid="206">Let us slide into your DMs.</strong><!-- react-text: 207 --> <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="208" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/newsletter/subscribe?sourceCode=articlelink"><!-- react-text: 209 -->Sign up for the <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="210">Teen Vogue</em><!-- react-text: 211 --> daily email<!-- /react-text --></a><!-- react-text: 212 -->.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p data-reactid="213"><strong data-reactid="214"><!-- react-text: 215 -->Want more from <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="216">Teen Vogue</em><!-- react-text: 217 -->? Check this out:<!-- /react-text --></strong><!-- react-text: 218 --> <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="219" href="https://www.teenvogue.com/story/blackpink-first-female-k-pop-group-to-play-coachella-2019">BLACKPINK Will Be the First Female K-Pop Group to Play Coachella</a></p>, <p data-reactid="331"><!-- react-text: 332 -->\xa9 <!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 333 -->2019<!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 334 --> Cond\xe9 Nast. [<p>Going into Sober January or a dry month can be daunting. If you're used to having a few drinks to loosen you up on dates or at social occasions, giving up that crutch can definitely be intimidating. But spending some time sober can actually be incredibly beneficial \u2014\xa0it can help your mood, self-esteem, health, and even your love life. You may just need to get used to <a class="E" href="https://www.glamour.com/story/things-you-learn-from-sober-dating" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">doing sober activities</a> with friends first.  </p>, <p>"Inevitably, Dry January will make you work on<a class="E" href="https://www.bustle.com/p/how-dry-january-benefits-your-dating-life-according-to-experts-7805416"> feeling comfortable with yourself </a>and your own self-esteem," <a class="E" href="http://rabbibregman.com/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Shlomo Zalman Bregman</a>, Rabbi, matchmaker, and relationship expert, tells Bustle. "Look, nobody is for everybody. This is part of life! There is no person on the planet \u2014 past or present \u2014 who is or was universally liked. So you might as well be yourself, sober and all \u2014 because the ideal partner for you will LOVE the person that you actually are!"</p>, <p>But still, it can be a tricky learning curve. If you're feeling a little <a class="E" href="https://www.bustle.com/p/how-dry-january-a-month-without-drinking-affects-your-body-7842987">nervous about dating sober</a>, you can try just spending more time socializing without alcohol. There are plenty of sober date ideas that you can do with friends this January to help ease you into being social without drinking. Here are some fun ideas to get you started. </p>, <p>Just because you're not drinking alcohol doesn't mean you can't drink. Going to a juice bar feeling <em>incredibly </em>wholesome, but it still allows you to try some interesting flavors \u2014\xa0without the hangover. </p>, <p>A group workout can be a really fun way to spend an afternoon or evening, especially if there's a cooperative or team-working element. Pickup soccer games in the park, boxing classes, or even a yoga workshop can all offer plenty of interaction opportunities. </p>, <p>A great day date activity, heading out for a hike is a good, low-pressure social activity. If you're located in a city, you can find a park and start exploring. </p>, <p>Board games are always a fun group activity and, frankly, they can go a lot better without the alcohol. You can host the night and order take-out or have everyone bring some food and mocktails along. </p>, <p>Spas as a group are a blast, because not only are they relaxing and indulgent, but something about the vulnerability of sitting around sweating in a towel can really help people open up. Get ready for some deep talks. </p>, <p>A coffee shop is an easy afternoon activity \u2014\xa0and if you find one with a great food or cake selection, you may find that you wile away an entire day there. </p>, <p>Always wanted to try a live drawing class? Pottery? Get a big group to book into a class together and you'll be too busy to notice the lack of alcohol. </p>, <p>January has the opportunity for all sorts of sports, from skating and skiing to just getting on a sled. It's good, wholesome, fun for all \u2014 and it's a lot safer when you do it sober. </p>, <p>If you want your wits about you, going to an escape room sober is probably your best bet. It's a really fun group activity and you'll be amazing how the time will fly by. </p>, <p>Brunch is the ultimate friend date \u2014\xa0but this time, just skip the unlimited mimosas. They'll still be there in February, don't worry. </p>, <p>Unless you're used to stashing some vodka in your bag, movies are often an alcohol-free experience anyway. Plus, they're a great way to pass a chilly January evening. </p>, <p>If you're looking to pull back on your drinking this month, these friend dates are an easy way to get used to socializing sober \u2014\xa0and you might just feel more empowered and assured at the end of it. </p>]

[<p class="text">As the world rings in 2019, it is time to pick new outfits for a new year of dating, parties and celebrations.</p>, <p class="text">For the Chinese people, the Spring Festival is only a month away and the festive atmosphere has already become pervasive. To contrast with the dark, early nights and reflect the joy of the season, bright colors are always more preferable during this time of year.</p>, <p class="text">Many Chinese film stars, while appearing in public around the New Year, have been seen wearing pink. A number of celebrities including singer Wang Ju, who was shot to fame from the 2018 hit talent show \u201cProduce 101\u201d, actress Li Qin and Chang Chun-ning have all put on either pink coats or sports jackets, cardigans or one-piece dresses.</p>, <p class="text">Golden Horse winning actresses Zhou Dongyu and Ma Sichun have also shown up in pink dresses to commercial activities and private events.</p>, <p class="text">Meanwhile, Victoria's Secret angels, such as Alessandra Ambrosio, Karlie Kloss and Jasmine Tookes have all been spotted wearing pink, especially with accessories such as purses.</p>, <p class="text">During New York Fashion Week Spring/Summer 2019 in September last year, the Pantone Color Institute issued a \u201cColor Trend Report\u201d for the upcoming season, which featured a pink tone stylishly named \u201cSweet Lilac\u201d.</p>, <p class="text">In Chinese culture, as the upcoming lunar New Year is the Year of the Pig, it is expected that pink will become the trend for the next spring. Especially because Peppa Pig, the main character of the hit British animation, has already become an online phenomenon with her hair-dryer-looking face and the cute pink color.</p>, <p class="text">It's still not too late to pick your pink fashion items before the Spring Festival!</p>, <p style="text-align:center;">\n<a href="https://www.facebook.com/echinanews" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ecns.cn/part/2015/07/2015-07-23/U435P886T30D169F196DT20150723092203.jpg"/></a>\n<a href="http://twitter.com/Echinanews" target="_blank"><img src="http://www.ecns.cn/part/2015/07/2015-07-23/U435P886T30D169F203DT20150723092203.jpg"/></a>\n</p>, <p><a href="http://www.ecns.cn/hd/2018-05-07/detail-ifytxtex5087691.shtml">Outfits turn ordinary men into fashion stars</a></p>]

[<p>By<p><span class="author-name vcard fn author" itemprop="name"><a href="https://stupiddope.com/author/jessedaugherty/" rel="author" title="Posts by Jesse James">Jesse James</a></span> <span class="mvp-author-twit"><a class="twitter-but" href="thee_jessejames" target="_blank"><i class="fa fa-twitter fa-2"></i></a></span> <span class="mvp-author-email"><a href="mailto:hiphopsense82@gmail.com"><i class="fa fa-envelope-o fa-2"></i></a></span></p></p>, <p><span class="author-name vcard fn author" itemprop="name"><a href="https://stupiddope.com/author/jessedaugherty/" rel="author" title="Posts by Jesse James">Jesse James</a></span> <span class="mvp-author-twit"><a class="twitter-but" href="thee_jessejames" target="_blank"><i class="fa fa-twitter fa-2"></i></a></span> <span class="mvp-author-email"><a href="mailto:hiphopsense82@gmail.com"><i class="fa fa-envelope-o fa-2"></i></a></span></p>, <p>For fans of modern art, Jean-Michel Basquiat\u2019s work is certainly at the top of the list. Jean-Michel Basquiat\u2019s life and his work has been well documented and explored, but recently things got much more in-depth thanks to a commemorative book aptly dubbed, Jean-Michel Basquiat. According to Artnet News, one of the drawings by the renowned artist reveals hidden messages in invisible ink. New York-based art conservator Emily Macdonald-Korth found the unique details when inspecting Basquiat\u2019s Untitled (1981) for a client.</p>, <p>Macdonald-Korth analyzed the painting under UV and infrared lighting, eventually finding the invisible ink. Macdonald-Korth told Artnet News \u201cI start looking at this thing and I see these arrows,\u201d though the arrows disappeared upon turning the lights on. The piece includes two arrows drawn in what looked like black-light crayon, which are identical to other arrows drawn visibly on the canvas with red and black oil sticks. Macdonald-Korth added: \u201cI\u2019ve never seen anything like it,\u201d further commenting \u201cHe basically did a totally secret part of this painting.\u201d</p>, <p>While it\u2019s not clear if Basquiat intended to implement the invisible drawings, Macdonald-Korth did share that, \u201cthere\u2019s a history there, having something secret there,\u201d she said. \u201cHe must have been playing with a UV flashlight and thought, \u2018this is cool.\u2019 It really relates to his use of erasure.\u201d Give us your thoughts in the comments and stay tuned for more on this coming soon. Head over to <a href="https://news.artnet.com/art-world/basquiat-hid-secret-images-in-work-1422499">Artnet News</a> to read the full story immediately.</p>, <p></p>, <p>Writer, Music enthusiast, style aesthete, footwear aficionado &amp; streetwear hoarder. I also unofficially hold the record for most published blog posts!</p>, <p>Beer Holthuis is a graduate of the Design Academy Eindhoven, and he is creating something unique...</p>, <p>Looking for an interesting and unique way to light up the new year? Well for the...</p>, <p>The San Diego International Airport is now host to three permanent site-specific installations. [<p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="109"><!-- react-text: 110 -->The <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="111" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/topic/coachella">Coachella</a><!-- react-text: 112 --> 2019 lineup is nothing short of impressive, but there is one superstar who is probably not too happy about the final roster: <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="113" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/topic/kanye-west">Kanye West</a><!-- react-text: 114 -->.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="115"><!-- react-text: 116 -->It has been eight years since West last headlined Coachella, and for months, rumors swirled that he would be one of the headliners for two consecutive weekends in April 2019. However, once the lineup revealed the headliners to be <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="117" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/topic/childish-gambino">Childish Gambino</a><!-- react-text: 118 -->, Tame Impala, and <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="119" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/topic/ariana-grande">Ariana Grande</a><!-- react-text: 120 -->, it was clear that the rapper would not be at the top of the ticket or anywhere on the lineup at all, for that matter. Many speculate that is likely that Grande, who West recently feuded <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="121" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/story/kanye-west-ariana-grande">with</a><!-- react-text: 122 --> on Twitter, was the last-minute replacement for the rapper.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="123"><!-- react-text: 124 -->According to the <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="125"><a data-reactid="126" href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/01/02/kanye-west-will-not-perform-coachella-2019-stage-negotiations/">TMZ</a></em><!-- react-text: 127 --> report, sources close to the rapper feel that the stage designs in Indio are too Shakespearean (read: old) for someone as visionary as West. "These 40x60 stages are so archaic," <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="128">TMZ</em><!-- react-text: 129 --> reports the sources said. "It's the same type of stage on which Shakespeare's works were performed hundreds of years ago," they went on.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="130"><!-- react-text: 131 -->Now let's not devalue the inventive nature of those Elizabethan playhouses from the 16th century. Sure, the stages did not move and float above the air the way West's stage did on the <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="132">Saint Pablo</em><!-- react-text: 133 --> tour, but Shakespeare's Globe Theatre was a complex construction, with multiple galleries and fairly good seating options. Sounds like something somebody who once shouted, <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="134" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bINO64iDaeY">"I am Shakespeare in the flesh!"</a><!-- react-text: 135 --> on a national radio show would be into if given the option, but West reportedly finds the traditional stage setup "artistically limiting." <!-- /react-text --><em data-reactid="136">TMZ</em><!-- react-text: 137 --> also reports that the Coachella producer, Goldenvoice, refused to give into West's demands for a moving stage at the Indio festival, and West declined the offer to headline.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="138"><!-- react-text: 139 -->So far, 2019 is already shaping up to be a big year for the West family anyway, and with <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="140" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/story/kim-kardashian-hinted-her-fourth-child-is-a-boy">another baby on the way</a><!-- react-text: 141 -->, the rapper may need to take some of that Coachella energy and turn it toward designing a new wing in his house for the children.<!-- /react-text --></p>, <p class="article-paragraph" data-reactid="142"><strong data-reactid="143">Related:</strong><!-- react-text: 144 --> <!-- /react-text --><a data-reactid="145" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/story/kim-kardashian-kanye-west-fourth-child-via-surrogate">Kim Kardashian and Kanye West Are Reportedly Having a Fourth Child Via Surrogate</a></p>, <p class="tag-hed" data-reactid="166">Keywords</p>, <p class="dek" data-reactid="292">Stay connected.</p>, <p class="copyright-text" data-reactid="378"><!-- react-text: 379 -->\xa9 <!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 380 -->2019<!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 381 --> Cond\xe9 Nast. <p class="mol-para-with-font"><a href="/tvshowbiz/katy_perry/index.html" id="mol-cdd31810-0f73-11e9-a4ea-9f5b482c31a8" style="font-weight: bold;">Katy Perry</a> rocked an odd outfit choice for a date with beau Orlando Bloom on Wednesday night.</p>, <p class="mol-para-with-font">The couple has been in Aspen for the last week hitting the slopes by day and the town by night.</p>, <p class="mol-para-with-font">Cameras spotted the pair as they headed out for a bite to eat at Japanese hot spot Matsuhisa.</p>, <p class="imageCaption">Colorful: Katy Perry went for a unique and colorful look for a date night with Orlando Bloom in Aspen on Wednesday</p>, <p class="mol-para-with-font">Bundled up for the chilly Colorado weather, Katy donned a long furry coat made of panels of mint green, purple, pale pink, white and bright yellow fur.</p>, <p class="mol-para-with-font">Under the coat, which she left open, the Roar singer sported a baby pink crushed velvet slip dress over thick white ribbed tights and chunky Fila sneakers.</p>, <p class="mol-para-with-font">The 34-year-old topped off the mishmash of pastel hues with pink resin hoops and a sky blue pair of fur earmuffs [<p class="post-meta"><span class="date updated"><i class="icon-time"></i>Jan 03, 2019</span><span class="vcard author meta-user"><span class="fn"><i class="icon-user"></i><a href="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/author/bill-heuer/" rel="author" title="Posts by Bill Heuer">Bill Heuer</a></span></span><span class="meta-cat"><i class="icon-book"></i><a href="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/category/comic/comic-blog/" rel="category tag">Comic Editorials</a></span><span class="meta-comment last-meta"><a href="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/batman-beyond-48/#respond"><span class="dsq-postid" data-dsqidentifier="52240 http://thebatmanuniverse.net/?p=52240"><i class="icon-comments"></i>0</span></a></span></p>, <p><strong><img alt="" class="alignleft wp-image-52285" height="600" sizes="(max-width: 390px) 100vw, 390px" src="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/beyond-666x1024.jpg" srcset="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/beyond-666x1024.jpg 666w, http://thebatmanuniverse.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/beyond-195x300.jpg 195w, http://thebatmanuniverse.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/beyond-768x1181.jpg 768w, http://thebatmanuniverse.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/beyond.jpg 1280w" width="390"/>Overview:</strong> After searching tirelessly for the Joker following the destruction of the new Wayne Tower and killing thousands, Terry takes a moment to reconnect with Melanie &amp; discuss their relationship. After another bombing, Terry and Matt are called to action and come face to face with the new cybernetic Joker \u201cBeyond\u201d.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p><strong>Synopsis (spoilers ahead):</strong> After days of looking for the Joker, Batman feels as if he has searched the entire city. He decides to take a moment to spend time with Melanie. The pair mentions their history together and Melanie reaffirms her goal of continuing down the straight-and-narrow path away from her past criminal activities. The romantic moment is broken with the sudden arrival of Robin stating that another bombing has occurred by the hands of the Joker.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>Prior to Robin\u2019s arrival, a random joker known as \u201cCC\u201d walks into a joker novelty shop and reveals that he is on a suicide bomb mission for the Joker. To the horror of Bernie, the owner, the Joker via view screen tells him that he has to go because he has insulted the image of the Joker with his dressing up the Jokerz gang.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>Following the explosion, the Joker is with his \u201cThrowback\u201d gang and discusses his disdain for this Neo Gotham and the Batman Beyond. He expresses his need and desire to bring back the dark and gritty Gotham he remembers even if it means evolving his methods. Using a knife, he murders one of his gang due to his boring name (John) and assures him he will be helpful in his grand plan.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>Back in the present with Terry and Matt, they head across the city to investigate the suicide bombing. While in transit, the pair is attacked by the gang of Joker\u2019s \u201cthrowbacks\u201d. During the fight, Matt tries to pursue one of the gang into a building but is violently knocked back. Arriving at his side, Batman is shocked at the introduction of a cyborg hybrid mixed with the corpse of the joker \u201cJohnny\u201d announced by the Joker as Joker Beyond.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p><strong>Analysis:</strong> While a less action-packed issue this month, it was nice to take a moment to explore Terry\u2019s relationship with Melanie (even if just for a few panels). It could be very easy to leave out that plot line to make room for more action so the effort by the creative team here to bring us more quiet moments for the hero to balance his crime-fighting life with his personal life is much appreciated.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>Jurgens explores an almost time-displaced Joker which brought up some disturbing tactics. I say \u201calmost time-displaced\u201d as we still have not gotten additional information as to how the Joker is present in Neo Gotham at the same age as we are used to seeing him. That would be my only minor nitpick in that it would be nice to get some hints dropped as to how he is there. Again, a very minor critique of an otherwise solid issue.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p>The artwork by Brett Booth really helped bring the Joker\u2019s manic nature and behavior to the forefront and central focus of this issue. You can really feel his rage turn to gleeful joy in an instant even transitioning between two side by side panels. He also handled the quiet moments between Terry and Melanie very well in showing their intimacy and feelings for each other.</p>, <p>\xa0</p>, <p><strong>Final Thoughts:</strong> Overall, this issue was much more enjoyable compared to the last few of this arc. It captured the psychotic nature of the Joker brought into the future Gotham. Although not a lot of action nor any additional details into how the Joker is present in the future, it felt true to the characters ever-changing mood.</p>, <p align="center">The Batman Universe and all material contained \xa9 2008-Present. All promotional stills/artwork copyright by their respective intellectual property holders.</p>, <p align="center"><a href="http://thebatmanuniverse.net/contact-us" target="_blank" title="Contact Us">Contact Us</a></p>]

[<p data-elm-loc="1">Daryl Dragon, the cap-wearing \u201cCaptain\u201d of Captain &amp; Tennille who teamed with then-wife Toni Tennille on such easy-listening hits as \u201cLove Will Keep Us Together\u201d and \u201cMuskrat Love,\u201d died Jan. 2 at a hospice center in Prescott, Ariz. He was 76.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="2">The cause was renal failure, said spokesman Harlan Boll. Tennille was by his side.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="3">\u201cHe was a brilliant musician with many friends who loved him greatly. I was at my most creative in my life, when I was with him,\u201d Tennille said in a statement. Mr. Dragon and Tennille divorced in 2014 after nearly 40 years of marriage, but they remained close. Tennille had moved back to Arizona to help care for him.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="4">Mr. Dragon and Tennille met in the early 1970s and soon began performing together, with the ever-smiling Tennille singing and the dourer Mr. Dragon on keyboards. He would later serve as Captain &amp; Tennille\u2019s producer.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="5">Their breakthrough came in 1975 when they covered the bouncy Neil Sedaka-Howard Greenfield song <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_QNEf9oGw8o" title="www.youtube.com">\u201cLove Will Keep Us Together.\u201d</a></p>, <p data-elm-loc="6">Sedaka and Greenfield, a top hitmaking team in the late 1950s and early 1960s, were nearing the end of their partnership and had written \u201cLove Will Keep Us Together\u201d as an ode to their longtime bond. Sedaka himself recorded the song, released it as a single in France and included it on his 1974 album \u201cSedaka\u2019s Back.\u201d</p>, <p data-elm-loc="8">Captain &amp; Tennille\u2019s version, slightly faster and funkier than the original, wasn\u2019t Mr. Dragon\u2019s first choice as a single. He had favored a cover of Beach Boy Bruce Johnston\u2019s \u201cI Write the Songs,\u201d which in 1976 became a signature hit for Barry Manilow.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="9">But \u201cLove Will Keep Us Together\u201d topped the charts in the summer of 1975. It won a Grammy for record of the year and not only made Captain &amp; Tennille stars but helped further revive Sedaka\u2019s career. In October 1975, his single \u201cBad Blood\u201d hit No. 1. Sedaka <a href="https://twitter.com/neilsedaka/status/1080603656507002886" title="twitter.com">tweeted Wednesday</a> that Mr. Dragon was \u201ca great musician, keyboard player and friend for over 40 years. He took \u2018Love Will Keep Us Together,\u2019 made it his own with the magic of his playing and her incredible voice.\u201d</p>, <p data-elm-loc="10">Meanwhile, Captain &amp; Tennille \u2014 known early on as the Captain &amp; Tennille \u2014 followed with a mix of covers such as <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xBYV_7a0FQs" title="www.youtube.com">\u201cMuskrat Love\u201d</a> and <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QpKqvdamEW4" title="www.youtube.com">\u201cShop Around\u201d</a> and original songs, including Tennille\u2019s ballad <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6ORUZxO0tw0" title="www.youtube.com">\u201cDo That to Me One More Time,\u201d</a> which hit No. 1 in 1980. They also briefly starred in their own television variety show before their careers faded in the 1980s.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="11">Over the past 30 years, they continued to perform and work together on occasion, with more recent albums including \u201cThe Secret of Christmas,\u201d from the mid-2000s.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="12">Daryl Frank Dragon was born in Los Angeles on Aug. 27, 1942. His father, Carmen Dragon, was a conductor and composer who won an Oscar for the 1944 movie musical \u201cCover Girl\u201d; his mother, Eloise Dragon, was a singer.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="14">Mr. Dragon, himself a classically trained musician, played keyboards with the Beach Boys beginning in the late 1960s and was dubbed \u201cthe Captain\u201d by singer Mike Love, who noted Mr. Dragon\u2019s fondness for sea captain\u2019s caps. Tennille briefly worked with the Beach Boys as a backup singer.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="15">Survivors include an older brother.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="16">In 2016, Tennille published \u201c<a href="https://read.amazon.com/kp/embed?asin=B01DAF6YII&amp;preview=newtab&amp;linkCode=kpe&amp;ref_=cm_sw_r_kb_dp_OfNlCbNHJRHFV&amp;tag=thewaspos09-20" title="read.amazon.com">Toni Tennille: A Memoir</a>,\u201d in which she alleged that their marriage was far removed from their cheerful hits. They were married in 1975, but Tennille recalled that their marriage was announced in advance \u2014 and to their surprise \u2014 by the record company.</p>, <p data-elm-loc="17">Tennille would allege that the couple suffered from lack of intimacy and blamed it on what she described as Mr. Dragon\u2019s \u201cvery, very difficult family\u201d and \u201cfamous but overbearing father.\u201d</p>, <p data-elm-loc="18">\u201cI kept trying and trying and thinking I could bring this man who has so much to give into the light,\u201d she told NBC\u2019s \u201cToday\u201d show in 2016. \u201cI wanted him to experience the joy that I had with my very loving family.\u201d</p>, <p data-elm-loc="19"><strong><info>\u2014 Associated Press</info> </strong></p>, <p data-elm-loc="20">Read more <b><a [<p>Pro wrestler Anthony Bowens came out as bisexual in 2017 but the 28-year-old now says he identifies as gay. </p>, <p>Bowens came out for the second time in a YouTube video titled \u201cCOMING OUT\u2026 again\u201d with his boyfriend Michael Pavano. </p>, <p>\u201cThe main purpose of this video is to tell everybody that I prefer to be labeled now as gay. There\u2019s going to be \u2018thank you, it\u2019s great that you\u2019re being open and honest and we love you\u2019, there\u2019s going to be the \u2018well, we knew that\u2019 and there\u2019s going to be the \u2018bi now gay later\u2019 people,\u201d Bowens says in the video. </p>, <p>He continued: \u201cI really didn\u2019t have <g class="gr_ gr_16 gr-alert gr_gramm gr_inline_cards gr_disable_anim_appear Grammar only-del replaceWithoutSep" data-gr-id="16" id="16">a thought</g> of men until maybe midway through high school, towards the latter end, I had a dream about one of my friends. And\u2026but after that <g class="gr_ gr_17 gr-alert gr_gramm gr_inline_cards gr_disable_anim_appear Punctuation only-ins replaceWithoutSep" data-gr-id="17" id="17">dream</g> I was like, \u2018Ooh. Something\u2019s different here.\u2019 And I kept having more of them\u2026and then I identified myself then as liking both genders. I came out as bisexual.\u201d</p>, <p>Bowens says at the time identifying as bisexual \u201cwas a very real thing\u201d and that he chose the label because he didn\u2019t know much about the LGBT community.</p>, <p> \u201cAs you get older, your viewpoints change. The way you look at the world changes, the way you look at yourself changes. Specifically more so in the past couple of months, this past year, I was looking at some old articles of mine because I was coming up with a new character for my wrestling career. And the articles kept labeling me as \u2018bisexual\u2019, and it was kind of annoying me that they had to continually put what I was, I couldn\u2019t just be a professional wrestler, I was the \u2018bisexual pro wrestler\u2019 but I just wasn\u2019t identifying with that term anymore,\u201d Bowens says.</p>, <p>Bowens publicly came out as bisexual in 2017 after his teammates found a video Pavano posted on YouTube of the couple doing \u201cThe Laughing Challenge.\u201d</p>, <p>Watch below. </p>, <p><a href="https://www.washingtonblade.com/tag/anthony-bowens/" rel="tag">Anthony Bowens</a><a href="https://www.washingtonblade.com/tag/michael-pavano/" rel="tag">Michael Pavano</a></p>, <p></p>]
[<p>\n<div class="field field-name-field-blog-subtitle field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">\n<p>Cameron Dallas later posted his mug shot on social media and claimed the alleged incident occurred in self-defense \u2014 all while the photo racked up thousands of likes, retweets and comments on Twitter and Instagram.\xa0</p> </div>\n</p>, <p>Cameron Dallas later posted his mug shot on social media and claimed the alleged incident occurred in self-defense \u2014 all while the photo racked up thousands of likes, retweets and comments on Twitter and Instagram.\xa0</p>, <p>Leave it to a social media sensation to somehow flip a story about his felony assault charges into an internet joke session around his mug shot.</p>, <p>Cameron Dallas was arrested on a felony charge of second-degree assault on Saturday, police in Aspen, Colorado said in a press release. He\xa0reportedly broke another man\u2019s nose after hitting him in the face.</p>, <p>An ambulance was called to the Hyatt Residences Grand Aspen at around 5 a.m. to treat an unidentified man who was bleeding from facial injuries he\u2019d sustained.</p>, <p>The alleged victim told police that he\u2019d been assaulted. Authorities later took Dallas, who was staying at the same hotel at the time, into custody.</p>, <p>Aspen Police Sgt. Rick Magnuson confirmed to\xa0<a href="https://www.aspentimes.com/news/internet-star-cameron-dallas-arrested-aspen-charged-felony-assault/">The Aspen Times</a> that Dallas was arrested and charged over the alleged face-breaking incident.</p>, <p>Dallas was released after posting $5,000 bond and is due to return to court on Jan. 22, police said.</p>, <p>After being released, Dallas took to\xa0<a>Twitter</a>\xa0on Monday and did what people like him do best: He used social media to influence the conversation surrounding the episode through shareable \u2014 which in most cases means humorous \u2014 content. Dallas rose to fame using the now defunct Vine app, and he has since built a considerable fanbase via YouTube and Netflix, which produces the docu-series in which he stars, \u201cChasing Cameron.\u201d</p>, <p>In a tweet, Dallas suggested to his 16 million followers his arrest was a matter of self-defense.</p>, <p>\u201cUnfortunately sometimes in life you find yourself in a situation where you have to protect yourself and the people you care about, have a safe and happy new year, 2019 is going to be an amazing one,\u201d he wrote.</p>, <p dir="ltr" lang="en">Unfortunately sometimes in life you find yourself in a situation where you have to protect yourself and the people you care about, have a safe and happy new year, 2019 is going to be an amazing one. <a href="https://t.co/VlYur8qyPU">pic.twitter.com/VlYur8qyPU</a>\u2014 Cameron Dallas (@camerondallas) <a href="https://twitter.com/camerondallas/status/1079885695899090944?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">December 31, 2018</a></p>, <p>The text, however, appeared to be completely overshadowed by the booking photo that accompanied it. The picture shows the 24-year-old internet personality clad in neon orange prison garments and flashing a knowing smirk.</p>, <p>Dallas has seemingly succeeded in getting his followers to focus solely on his silly prison portrait rather than the whole felony assault thing the photo stems from.</p>, <p>The shot has been retweeted more than 6,600 times and has received 60,000 favorites. Further, a parsing of the comments posted below the tweet indicates what\u2019s on people\u2019s minds: \u201c<a href="https://twitter.com/CharielleCruz16/status/1080313602886688769">His smile says \u2018yep I did it, watcha gonna do.\u2019 Haha love you Cam</a>;\u201d \u201c<a href="https://twitter.com/NCKIJunior/status/1079960397971546113">Ah now more attracted now that he has a mugshot</a> (sic);\u201d \u201c<a href="https://twitter.com/PaytonWasserman/status/1079895047821316097">I\u2019m making this a t-shirt the caption and everything.</a>\u201d</p>, <p>Dallas also shared his mugshot on\xa0<a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/BsEg9n5gXnj/">Instagram</a>, where the photo garnered more than one million likes in a matter of days.</p>, <p><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>\r\n
